The terms of office of the officials of the local County Chamber of Commerce have expired and should be re-elected in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law promulgated by the National Government. On the afternoon of the tenth, the votes were counted in public, and the fifteen elected executive committee members were Cai Guangyao, Shu Bao Shan, Zhou Tingzhen, Zhang Fucun, Pan Guoping, Zhang Ruoshui, Yang Zhimin, Ding Zhouzhi, Xie Jingshan, Wu Shengyong, Yang Wenhua, Tang Zhimin, Wu Zai Su, Shen Si Nan, and Wang Zuoting. The supervisory committee members were Du Yingchang, Feng Shouhu, Wang Xianglin, Hong Songqiao, Fang Zhongqiao, and Wang Liangqing.

Fengxian

County Magistrate's Illegal Handling of Escaped Prisoners

The Fengxian prisoners' escape was recorded in this newspaper's major events. Later, County Magistrate Shen executed two recaptured escaped prisoners, Wang A Bao and Zhang A Da, in the name of the County Government. The Executive Committee of the First District Party Department of the county stated that since County Magistrate Shen took office, he has neither improved the local area nor competed to destroy it, and the people's resentment is very deep. This time, the execution of the two prisoners did not announce the charges, nor did it request approval from the Provincial Government. It was indeed a dictatorial execution, which was a private and playful act. Murderer. A special request was made to the County Executive Committee to investigate the matter thoroughly. The text roughly said: According to the investigation, as of July 17th, a total of 58 people had escaped. 26 of them were killed on the spot or drowned, 14 were recaptured (including two who have been executed). 18 are at large. Another one, A Mei, who sold cakes, was mistakenly killed. However, on the morning of July 22nd, the recaptured escaped prisoner Wang A Bao was escorted to the left side of the Sanguantang Temple and executed by shooting in the name of the County Government. According to outside rumors, Wang was the chief culprit. On the afternoon of the 22nd, another escaped prisoner, Zhang A Da, who had been shot and wounded, was captured and interrogated. On the morning of the 23rd, he was also carried on a palm mat to the back of the First Water Patrol Team and executed by shooting by order of the County Government. According to outside rumors, Zhang was also the chief culprit. This time, the County Government resolutely acted according to military law, or because the two prisoners' crimes were serious and the law was unforgivable. However, as of the 27th, the charges against the two prisoners have not been announced, which has raised doubts about the legal principles: (1) If County Magistrate Shen concurrently serves as a military judge, why have the charges not been announced for many days after the recaptured escaped prisoners were executed? (2) The County Government has no power to execute prisoners dictatorially. If it is believed that the prisoners should be sentenced to death, it must also telegraph the Provincial Government for instructions. Then, its unauthorized killing of prisoners is inevitably a private act and a play on the law. In his mind, he disregards the decrees of the National Government and the orders of the Provincial Government. His absurd behavior is not what an official under the Qingbai banner should do.

Busiest Are Running Around Requesting Joint Issuance

The time for the issuance of busy silver vouchers above the village level in this county coincides with the fifth and sixth months of the year, when there are widespread famines. Most businesses are unable to respond due to livelihood constraints. Some even owe until the winter grain shipment before settling. However, the supervisors in charge of collecting taxes have set deadlines that cannot be delayed, causing the micro-economic villages to be in a difficult position. Therefore, the village leaders, represented by Jiang Sanjing of Fang 13, submitted a statement of the previous situation, requesting that the busy silver vouchers above the village level be issued jointly with the busy opening of the village below. However, it is understood that the county government believes that there are indeed many valid reasons stated in this case, but because the case has been opened, it is not convenient to change it. Therefore, yesterday, it was approved to continue to follow the previous example and pay according to the deadline.

More Bandits Arriving at Qianjiawei

Qianjiawei was originally a place where bandits hid. Suddenly, on the evening of the seventh, more than a hundred bandits arrived, spreading all over the streets. They were all armed and were said to have come from Luwan Temple in Zhejiang Province because the bandits had received advance notice that the Xincang Provincial Security Team was coming to suppress them. It was also heard that the anti-smuggling team discovered many bandits in the southeast of Liujia Yanqiao the other day. The two sides opened fire for a short time, and the bandits all fled. When the fire broke out, an old woman surnamed Mou, who was drying sauce on the scene, was hit in the abdomen by a stray bullet and has now died.

Suzhou

Petition to Change the Method of Collecting Busy Grain

The Department of Finance of Wu County approved the collection of various donations with the busy grain for the 19th year, including a local subsidy fee of 45 cents per tael of busy silver, a county road construction mu tax of 50 cents, a Jun Song fee of 20 cents per tael of less busy silver, a county public security fee of 35 cents, a county road construction mu tax of 50 cents, and the following with each stone of grain, a local subsidy fee of 1 yuan, a county public security fee of 70 cents, a security group fee of 50 cents, an education mu tax of 1.3 yuan, an agricultural improvement mu tax of 24 cents, and a local subsidy mu tax of 1.115 yuan. The total is 3.92225 yuan per tael of provincial and county taxes for busy silver, 3.19225 yuan per tael of less busy silver, and 10.115 yuan per stone of grain. However, the collection date has always been the busy silver first, and then the less busy grain is collected at a fixed date. Now the Finance Bureau plans to change the plan to collect the less busy grain at the same time and has submitted a request to the department for instructions.

Telegram to Qidong Bandit Police

The Jiangsu High Court received a telegram from Xia Yunqing, the county magistrate of Qidong County, stating that more than 100 Communist bandits arrived in the county on the evening of the 8th and carried out riots. First, they completely released more than 100 prisoners held in two prisons. Then, they set fire to the two prisons. When the Suzhou land covering industry had a labor dispute, it took three months to resolve. Now the county party has forwarded it to the county government to be reviewed by the General Chamber of Commerce, and Zheng and others submitted another petition to the provincial office yesterday, requesting the county to follow suit.

Jiangyin

Banditry in Shizhuang Town, Many Deaths from Robbery of Weapons

Shizhuang Town in Taohua Township, west of the county, is located at the junction of Cheng and Wu and has long been a place for bandits to come and go. After County Magistrate Li led a team to the countryside to suppress them the other day, the bandits harbored resentment. At about 1:00 AM on the 9th, they gathered more than 200 bandits, armed with guns, first went to Ma Kou Li Village and searched the home of Jin Shanghang, the former director of the township administration, and shot Jin Shanghang in the buttocks, injuring his urethra and endangering his life. His aunt, niece, and nephew, Jin Bangjun, were all shot. Jin Chengqing and Jin Yuanlin, wealthy households in the village, were shot and killed, and an old woman also died. Then they went to Shizhuang Street to rob the Public Security Sixth Branch Police Station, losing two guns and killing a police officer named Wang Hengxing. Baofeng Rice Shop, Xiangji Hotel, and Jin Yuelai Longyuan Tea Shops were all robbed. After the bandits robbed, they went to Guanzhuang to burn it down. At that time, the police team in the city had been ordered to go to the countryside and came from Huangtan and other places. They encountered the bandits and the two sides fought fiercely. The police team was outnumbered and retreated to Ligang. In the afternoon, they hurried to the city to report to the county government. In the evening, County Magistrate Li led a team to the countryside himself to suppress the bandits and to survey the scene where Jin Shanghang and others were injured. Five people were sent to the Eastern Outer Gospel Hospital for treatment.

Security Team Detains Robbers

Jin Jiarui, the head of the first squad of the East Outer District Security Team, reported that the robbers Zhu Yuanlang and Zhao Laosi, etc., who were involved in the robbery case of Zhou Xiaogao's house in Fangjia Pond, were hiding in Wangfu. He led a team to arrest them and escorted them to the First District Regiment Headquarters. Because it is now a time of martial law, they are under the jurisdiction of Commander Yang of the Fortress for interrogation.

Commander Yang Issues a Proclamation to Maintain Order

Commander Yang of the Fortress issued a proclamation yesterday, saying: "For the purpose of the proclamation, I received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Jiang of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, and I understand the two telegrams from Kai Zhi and Hao Shen. The wounded soldiers in the Twenty-fifth Rear Hospital are causing trouble, and their behavior in the area is illegal. If they are not strictly cracked down on, there will be concerns about the local security. Now, all the garrisoned military police in Cheng County are under the command of Commander Yang to guard the hospital and maintain order. The commander shall plan and allocate accordingly. If the wounded soldiers continue to cause trouble arbitrarily and refuse to obey orders, the commander shall be allowed to handle them at his own discretion. In addition to sending telegrams separately, a special telegram is sent for compliance." Upon receiving this order, I checked that it is the duty of soldiers to fight against rebellion, sacrifice for the party and the country, and it is their duty. Now that they are injured and recuperating in the hospital, they should abide by military discipline and maintain their reputation. However, some ignorant wounded soldiers are acting recklessly in groups of three or five, causing trouble in the area, and even using guns to rob guns and become thugs. Such actions are indeed abominable. After this proclamation, if any wounded soldiers do not abide by military discipline and act lawlessly, they will be severely punished once they are caught, and even punished by military law. This commander's words are the law, do not say that I did not warn you! Obey and do not violate, be sure to be sure.

Wuxi

Suspects Arrested in Sunxiang Robbery Case

Sun Leikui's family in Shangsunxiang, Yinqiao Township, District 16 (Wan'an City), County was robbed and beaten the other night. The matter has been reported to the county for investigation. Captain Zhu immediately sent Liao Dajin, the head of the detective team, to lead the detectives to the countryside for investigation. At about 6:00 PM that afternoon, they were transported by car to the city and escorted to the team headquarters for interrogation. After an interrogation, they were transferred to the county for questioning.

Perpetrator in Boat With Four Deaths Case Executed by Shooting

Xu Jianshan, a villager in Xuxiang, Kaihua Township, Xi County, hired Shao Qiaosheng's boat in the spring of this year to transport money, rice, and sundries to Dongshan, Dongting, Taihu Lake. On the way, he was robbed and Xu Jianshan and the boatman Shao Qiaosheng's father and son were killed, a boat with four lives. Later, Ni Gusheng, the captain of the Second Water Police District Detective Team, purchased an informant named Qian Genbao and assisted the police officers in arresting the main perpetrators in this case, Zhao Shansheng, Chen Jisheng, Qin Da Wang, and others in the Shuibei area of Guangfu, Su County, as well as two suspects, Qian Guanbao and Wang Qiaosheng, and three stolen boats. There were several women and children on the boat. After repeated trials, Zhao Shansheng and others confessed that on April 22 of this year, in the Jiaozui area of Taihu Lake, they and Chen Changsheng, Chen Jinsheng, Liu Fucai, and others, who were at large, drove two fishing boats to chase and rob Xu Jianshan's boat. The boatman Shao Qiaosheng fought back with the helm handle and fell into the lake because he used too much force. Zhao used a pole to stab Shao into a hole and sink him to his death. Then, Chen Jinsheng and Liu Fucai, who were at large, used poles to poke holes in Xu Jianshan and Shao Qiaosheng's sons, Guoqing and Qiqing, and sink them to their deaths. County Magistrate Sun reported the situation to the provincial government, and on the afternoon of the other day (9th), he received a telegram from the provincial government approving the execution of the bandit Zhao Shansheng, Yang Jisheng, and Qin Da Wang. County Magistrate Sun immediately signed the order to bring the bandits to verify their identities and tie them to the South School Field for execution by shooting.

Director of Finance Bureau Resigns

Chen Liangdong, Director of the Finance Bureau, resigned because the autumn harvest in Xi County was poor last year, and the spring and summer cocoons and wheat were poor this year, resulting in an unusually low tax revenue. Compared with previous years, there was a large shortage. It was difficult to pay the provincial funds, and the county funds were also heavily burdened. Yesterday, he submitted a special report to the department in person to explain the difficulties and request to resign. At the same time, Chen Zhanru, the chairman of the County Fund Management Office, also submitted a resignation to the county government, saying that the local expenses were in huge deficit and on the verge of bankruptcy, while the funds to be paid were still coming in, making it difficult to cope. He also requested that Director Hua Shaochun temporarily maintain the office affairs.

Rickshaw Guild Refuses to Give Subsidy

The County General Labor Union Consolidation Committee previously stated that the local Rickshaw Association had promised to subsidize the union's regular expenses by 100 yuan per month, which had not been paid for two years. Now, the union is experiencing financial difficulties and has submitted a request to the county government to recover the funds. County Magistrate Sun immediately sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to inform the union. Now, the Chamber of Commerce has received a reply from the rickshaw stating that the Rickshaw Association has been reorganized and the guild has decided that all unreasonable distributions cannot be recognized. The health and medical expenses of the rickshaw pullers have also been specially contracted with Tongren Hospital to be responsible for treating all rickshaw pullers who go to the hospital free of charge. Now that commerce is declining, there are no surplus funds to subsidize any external organizations. The Chamber of Commerce has reported the situation to the county government.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Yahe Town

More than a dozen bandits arrived in Yahe Town, west of Wu County, at about 11:00 PM on the 8th. They were wearing short white cloth shirts and black Xiangyun gauze pants, all holding box guns and pistols. Because Wang Kunsheng's family did not get a large amount of property, they also stripped his child, Zhang Bao, naked and took him away. The city police brigade headquarters heard the news and Captain Chen Daxix immediately sent Wang, the deputy captain, and Liu, the special affairs officer, to lead the team to encircle and arrest them. At about 4:00 AM on the morning of the 9th, they discovered a suspicious person while encircling and searching. After arresting him, he claimed to be Wang Dajiang. He was taken to Zheng Xiqi, a Liaoning native in Yahe, who greeted Wang Da, and he was also arrested. Then, Liu Laoer, a person who looked at wood rafts along the canal, was also arrested and taken to Yahe. The victim of the robbery identified Wang Da as the perpetrator who had bound the staff and kidnapped Wang Kunsheng's child that night. The Massacre in Makou Village, Cheng County and Shizhuang

Makou Village in Jiangyin County is very close to the boundary of Wujin County. On the 2nd of this month, Jin Shanghang, the former director of the Taohua Township Administration, led many people to Guanzhuang and other places to arrest bandits. Therefore, the bandits harbored resentment. In addition, Li Leng, the county magistrate of the county, and Li Zonggang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, had led a team to Guanzhuang to arrest the bandit leader Liu Hongxi in the Xia Gang robbery case. Therefore, the bandits hated the people of Makou Village even more for guiding the capture. At dawn on the 9th, more than 100 bandits, each wearing white short shirts and pants, led a military horn to Makou Village and opened fire to demonstrate. Then, they wantonly shot and killed people and did the same in nearby Shizhuang. However, they did not rob property. Then, the Xishiqiao Merchant Group and the Public Security Bureau rushed to suppress them. They encountered the bandits on the way and the two sides opened fire. The bandits ran out of ammunition and began to disperse. Two bandits were killed by the police. In Makou Village and Shizhuang, there were many deaths and injuries. According to investigations, the deceased were Yang Dinggui's wife, Jin Ronglin, Jin Ronghai, Jin Qisheng, Jin Chengqing, Jin Qianqing, Jin Yuqing, and others. The injured are being sent to the hospital for treatment.

Interrogation of Sea Bandit Forced Occupancy of Women Case

The county sent personnel to Haimen to welcome and bring back the sea bandit Liu Anbang the other day. At 11:00 AM on the morning of the other day, the victim Shen Xu came to the government to report the case. Cen, the trial officer, interrogated her. The woman stated that she was 25 years old and lived in Hupu. Her husband's name was Yunsheng and he supported a boat in Shanghai. She had a daughter named Xiao Erzi, who was seven years old. In the autumn of last year, Liu Anbang and others came to her house to rob her and raped her. Then, she was kidnapped to the boat for three months. In the spring of this year, she was rescued after the police arrested Liu Anquan, who had been shot to death. On May 28, Liu Anbang came to rob her again. She opened the door and escaped, and Liu went into the room and snatched her daughter. Now that the case has been solved, she is asking for her daughter to be returned to her. Then, Xiao Erzi, who was seven years old, was interrogated. The official ordered Xiao Erzi to identify what Shen Xu called her. Xiao Erzi replied that she called her "Mom." Then, Liu Anbang was interrogated and said that he was 46 years old and from Yancheng. He asked his wife Shen Xu to request the court to investigate the matter clearly so that he could die in peace. The official ordered Shen Xu to testify and still stated that she was not Liu's wife and was indeed forced to occupy her. Then, Shen Han was interrogated and said that her son's name was Yunsheng and he married a daughter-in-law named Qian. The official ordered Shen Han to make a statement to prove that Xiao Erzi would be handed over to Shen Xu to take back. Liu Anbang was taken back for further investigation.

Problem of Adding Rickshaws for Rickshaw Pullers

The local Rickshaw Pullers' Union submitted a proposal to add rickshaws last month and was approved by the County Party Department to send a letter to the county. At 1:00 AM on August 8th, the local Communist bandits colluded with approximately five to six hundred bandits and launched a surprise attack on the county seat in three routes. Police Officer Robs Pig Buyer

On the 7th, Tai Xingzhu, a pig buyer, Ding Shaolan, was carrying 283 yuan when he returned to his hometown from Shenyang. He landed at Xingang and walked home. When he reached the Shengjia Wei of Henan, Jijiashi, two people resembling soldiers came face to face and held a box cannon, ordering him to stop. They grabbed all the money Ding was carrying. Afterwards, Ding went to Captain Wang of the County Police Detachment stationed in Jijiashi to report the incident and said that the two people looked very much like the police officers of your team. Upon receiving the report, Captain Wang immediately gathered all the team members to let him identify them. Ding pointed out that Zhu Guangyou, a second-class police officer of the Second Detachment, was indeed one of the perpetrators. Captain Wang searched him and found 144 yuan of silver, which he confessed to conspiring with Xue Rongquan, a second-class police officer of the same team, to commit the robbery. Xue had already divided the money and fled. Captain Wang believed that the police officers were soldiers and were responsible for protecting the safety of the people. They dared to commit such illegal acts, which was a heinous crime. He escorted Zhu Guangyou to the city and sent Sun Zhonglin, a special affairs officer of the Third Detachment, overnight with Chen, a special affairs officer of the Second Detachment, to strictly investigate and arrest the fleeing police officer Xue Rongquan. Last night, he caught Xue at the Xinshunxing Hotel. Xue was entertaining prostitutes and found 131 yuan of stolen silver. He was immediately escorted to the county. After being interrogated by Investigator Yin, he was handcuffed and imprisoned to await legal action.

Zhenjiang

Two More County Chiefs Accused

Yesterday, the Jiangsu Provincial Government received a complaint from Huang Housheng and others, citizens of Chongming County, accusing County Chief Feng of disregarding the law and mistreating the people, urging the dispatch of personnel for thorough investigation. Additionally, Hu Yannong and others, citizens of Gaoyou County, accused Zhou Zhendong, the Public Security Bureau Chief of the county, of deliberately violating provincial orders and extorting money from the villagers, requesting severe punishment. After receiving the complaints, the Provincial Government yesterday ordered the Civil Affairs Department to conduct thorough investigations separately, pending review and handling.

Over a Hundred Bandits Burn Nanqingshan

In Nanqingshan, a place in the western countryside of Zhenjiang County, about forty miles from the city, over a hundred bandits suddenly appeared the night before last. Armed with guns and weapons, they created a great disturbance. Families with some wealth were all robbed, and dozens of houses were burned down, totaling more than twenty families. The mother of villager Fu Jinhai, who is over sixty years old, somehow angered the bandits and was shot, a cruelty beyond description. By the time the military and police heard the news and went to pursue them, the bandits had already vanished without a trace.

Yangzhou

Ferry Manager Accused

The Second Sub-branch of the Third District Party Department in Guazhou Town of this county stated that the Pujin Ferry is jointly operated by Jiangdu, Yizheng, and Zhenjiang counties, with Zhenjiang as the main entity. It operates daily between Shierxu, Guazhou, Liuxu, and Zhenjiang, with only one ferry. Whenever repairs are needed, it is replaced with a red boat. However, this time, due to the collapse of the riverbank in Liuxu, the damage to the ferry has not been promptly repaired, nor has it been replaced with a red boat, causing great inconvenience to passengers. Furthermore, when the ferry was affected by the riverbank collapse in Liuxu, passengers fell into the water and drowned. The recovered bodies were not photographed or claimed. The manager of the ferry company, Lu Jinquan, disregarded this. Therefore, the District Party Department requested the County Party Department to consult the County Court for legal action.

Qingjiang

Part of the Xiba Anti-Smuggling Brigade Mutinies

Xiba is located in the third district of Huaiyin, on the south bank of the Yan River and the north bank of the Yellow River, stretching about four miles from east to west and one mile from north to south. There are eighteen or nineteen salt depots, serving as a storage and transit point for salt from northern Jiangsu. The salt authorities have always stationed a battalion or large brigade of anti-smuggling troops in the town to prevent salt smuggling. Currently, the First Brigade of the Huaihai Anti-Smuggling Water Police is stationed in the town, with its bases not in one place. One part of it is stationed near the Qianfu Salt Depot. Yesterday (the 7th) at 7 PM, this part of the water police suddenly mutinied. The local merchants and residents were immediately startled by the sound of gunfire and were terrified. In addition to the First Brigade of the Water Police, there were also patrol teams and salt escort teams stationed in the town. The Third Sub-bureau of the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau was also located in the town below Yangjia Wharf. Upon hearing the news, the Third Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, the patrol team, and the escort team also temporarily gathered to devise ways to defend and suppress the mutiny. Sub-bureau Chief Wu Yinchuan sent someone to report to the County Bureau in the county town and to the headquarters of the 266th Regiment of the 133rd Brigade of the garrison troops. Immediately, the police brigade of the Public Security Bureau and the Third Battalion of the 266th Regiment dispatched teams overnight to suppress the mutiny. The mutineers dared to resist and opened fire, and the two sides fought for about half an hour. One mutineer was killed and three were injured. The mutineers were defeated and fled to the north bank of the Yan River and the south bank of the Yellow River. Government troops pursued and suppressed them in separate directions. According to someone who came to the city this morning (the 8th) from Langshi Town on the north bank of the Yan River, about forty mutineering water police officers had been overtaken by government troops in Langshi, and the situation was serious as they were being rounded up. There was no news of other government troops pursuing the defeated mutineers arriving in the city. Public Security Bureau Chief Zhao Zhenhua and Police Brigade Chief Zhu Lianfang had also not yet arrived in the county town. As for the cause of the water police mutiny, there were many rumors. Some said that dozens of plainclothes ruffians came to rob, and the water police were accomplices. Others said that the water police had gone down the Yan River a few days ago to suppress bandits and disobeyed their superiors, and the superiors reported this to prepare for punishment, so they launched the mutiny first. The latter explanation was more widely accepted, and it was not without reason. Fortunately, when the mutiny began, all parties took early precautions, and the area did not suffer widespread destruction.

The Hangzhou-Shanghai long-distance telephone line was disconnected due to complex internal disagreements between the Zhejiang Long-Distance Telephone Management Office of the Ministry of Communications and the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau. This has been going on for nearly a month. This problem will be delayed indefinitely.

Trouble Caused by Wounded Soldiers Buying Goods in Jianqiao

At about 10 AM today (the 10th), several wounded soldiers from the rear army general hospital of the Jianqiao general headquarters went to the Yushengyong grocery store in Jianqiao town to buy perfume essence. Because they used the new double-horn coin of the 90th year of the Republic, the store refused to accept it, and the two sides argued. The local police were trying to resolve the situation, but they were dissatisfied, causing a major conflict. More and more wounded soldiers gathered, and some even snatched the police's weapons. The police fired a warning shot to defend themselves, but it accidentally injured five soldiers (it is said that one of them was seriously injured and may die). All the shops in the town closed their doors. The police station was also completely destroyed by the wounded soldiers, with losses of more than 2,000 yuan. Deputy Director Cai of the hospital was present to suppress the situation but was ineffective. He telegraphed the provincial government and the provincial capital's public security bureau. Chief Zhu of the Security Division and Director Yan of the Public Security Bureau dispatched a company of instructors and a team of joint military and police inspectors, led by Qi Xiaofeng and Wu Ding, to Jianqiao by car to suppress the situation and investigate the truth of the incident.

Mo Mengkao and others were responsible for raising funds. It is now known that the funds have been secured and construction is scheduled to begin at the end of the month. The design has been finalized, and the foundation will be built with cement, surrounded by iron chains.

The styles of the streets inside and outside Pinghu City are old and narrow. Bandits Who Enter Softly and Leave Forcefully

In Yejiabang, near Mayao Town in Huzhou, Ye Jing'an, a wealthy man, was robbed by seven or eight thieves around 2 AM on the night of the 31st of last month. They dug a hole in the western wall and entered, holding knives and sticks, with cloths covering their faces and speaking with local accents. They dragged Ye Jing'an out of bed, held a knife to his neck, and threatened him to hand over silver dollars. Ye repeatedly begged in vain. The bandits searched the rooms at will, looting clothes, jewelry, silk, and more, as well as over 400 silver dollars in cash, taking over an hour. Ye's family suffered losses of over 2,000 yuan this time.

Kaihua

Delineation of Boundaries Between Kaihua and Xiuning

The boundary dispute between Kaihua in Zhejiang Province and Xiuning in Anhui Province has been repeatedly surveyed but has not been resolved. When the Ministry of Interior sent a commission for surveying last year, Zhejiang Province stated that the unclear boundary had implications for all administrative matters, and it was originally intended to use the natural watershed of Majin Ridge as the boundary. The Ministry Commission also expressed approval. However, the issue was not finalized because the boundary survey regulations had not been promulgated, and the original situation was maintained. Now, another survey is about to take place. Upon hearing this, the people of Kaihua learned that one or two local bullies in Xiuning, disregarding the natural terrain and administrative convenience, were plotting to seize Kaihua's inherent territory to satisfy their desire for money. Public sentiment was aroused. It is reported that various people's organizations and legal groups are gathering and will make major representations. It is also reported that they have telegraphed the Ministry of Interior and the Provincial Government, vowing to fight to the death.

Britain Prepares to Welcome the Chinese Expeditionary Soccer Team

Banquet in the House of Commons... Meet with Strong Teams

(London Dispatch) The Chinese Expeditionary Soccer Team's round-the-world tour plan has been finalized on all sides. The team members are selected from strong teams in North China, Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Singapore. After arriving in Europe, the competition will be held in Vienna first, followed by Germany, Hungary, Switzerland, and other countries. It is planned to arrive in England around October 28th. Lord Frederick Walder decided to host a banquet for the Chinese team in the House of Commons as an official welcome from the British government.

The competition will be against the most elite amateur soccer teams in Britain, and the representative strong teams of England, Ireland, Scotland, and Wales will be carefully selected to

observe soccer skills with the Chinese Expeditionary Force and promote international friendship.

The Chinese team's accommodation headquarters in England are now planned in York, but they often go to London for leisure. The Ilford F.C. of the Amateur Championship has prepared a welcoming order and cordially welcomes the Eastern soccer guests.

Lord Walder and Reverend Denny Cole (Deputy Speaker of the House of Commons and President of the Ilford F.C.) have promised to do their best to help with material and spiritual assistance to the Chinese Expeditionary Force.

Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia Win Open Doubles Championship

Three to Two... Defeat Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang

丨 Consecutive Wins in the Last Three Sets 丨 Come From Behind 丨

The sensational Shanghai Open Doubles Tennis Championship has been in full swing since the start of the battle. The heroes took to the stage and competed with each other. Those who stood out in the final scene yesterday were Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia against Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang. The three, Qiu, Jiang, and Lin, are national players in the Chinese tennis world, and Zheng is also known for being handsome and promising. The final meeting of famous generals and heroes is not only consistent with the reputations of both sides, but also feels like a mutual wish fulfillment. In the midst of the battle, Qiu and Jiang unfortunately suffered a tragic defeat in the great cause that was about to be completed, while Lin and Zheng, who were worried about the impending failure, suddenly came up with unexpected success. One sorrow and one joy can be imagined. The result of the game was three to two, Lin and Zheng won. Referee: Shen Siliang.

A Once-in-a-Lifetime Opportunity

Both sides have outstanding skills and famous names. They have a considerable understanding of each other and mutual respect. However, because there is rarely a chance to compare, it is not easy to strongly distinguish their strengths. Since participating, they knew that there would be yesterday's meeting. It is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. The four players do not know whether they can meet again in the arena on this day next year. The opportunity is rare. How can the thousands of spectators enjoy the visual feast again and see the heroes of the world show their skills as they did yesterday? In short, yesterday's battle can be described as an unprecedented event in the history of Chinese tennis.

First Set... Eight to Ten

Ups and Downs

The famous generals stepped onto the stage with great power. High-pressure and low-pressure shots each have their own strengths. Lin Baohua served first, with formidable power. Zheng Zhaojia assisted as needed, with great success. Before long, the first game was easily obtained. When it came to Jiang Daozhang's serve, it was fierce and powerful, coupled with a good backhand, he won the second game. The third game belonged to Lin and Zheng, and the fourth game belonged to Qiu and Jiang. In short, the serving group, whether it was Lin and Zheng or Qiu and Jiang, benefited. Afterwards, ups and downs corresponded, such as one to one, two to two, three to three, four to four, five to five, becoming an unchanging rule. However, Lin and Zheng took the lead because of the first serve.

Failure to Fall into the Trap

After five-five, there was a sudden change. When Zheng served, Qiu and Jiang used tricks to take advantage of the enemy's unpreparedness and lobbed the ball to the rear. Zheng failed because of this, and the momentum of ups and downs was broken. Qiu and Jiang took the lead with six to five. Who knew that Qiu also lost because of a weak serve and became a six-six tie again. Lin Baohua showed his power with his serve and won a game with four straight wins, retaking the lead. Jiang Daozhang pounced on the sheep like a hungry tiger, and it was irresistible, becoming a seven-seven tie again. Qiu Feihai's smashes were excellent, and Jiang Daozhang's forehand and backhand dominated. Lin and Zheng were exhausted from running around and fell into the trap (Qiu and Jiang took the lead with eight to seven). However, in the subsequent game, Qiu and Jiang did not handle it properly and were taken away by Lin and Zheng again (eight-eight tie). In the seventeenth game, Lang used supernatural and unpredictable skills to beat the opponent and leave them at a loss. At that time, Lin's serve was unable to save the situation. In the eighteenth game, Qiu and Jiang frequently shot at Zheng with their superior momentum, so they were able to win the first set with a score of ten to eight, as shown on the left.

Second Set... Four to Six

One Breath

Lin and Zheng took advantage of the serve, and Zheng's pressure shot was quite skillful. Therefore, the two complemented each other, and the first game was taken for their own. In the second game, the ball flew back and forth in the middle of the field, and the mutual shooting in the air was a spectacle. Lin and Zheng were faster and took the upper hand. They won two games in one breath, and the future looked promising and optimistic.

Defeated Again

When Lin and Zheng were in high spirits, they were suddenly attacked by the opponent. Jiang's backhand and high-pressure shot were strong and powerful. The random shots were very impressive, and the net shots in a busy life were also wonderful. Coupled with Qiu's composure, before long, the two-two tie was heard in the arena. However, since then, the two sides have been equally matched in their skills, and it has been difficult to distinguish the male from the female. After another four games, they became four-four ties. Qiu and Jiang worked harder and their aura suddenly became stronger. Lin and Zheng were defeated again, failing with four to six. The score is shown on the left.

Third Set... Six to Two

Defeat the Strong First

Qiu and Jiang won two consecutive sets, and their momentum was so overwhelming that it was not difficult to swallow the four wastelands and sweep the universe, and the championship title also had a sense of who else could get it other than me. When the third set started, Qiu and Jiang took the lead again. Relying on the power of the smash and high pressure, they won the first and second games. The audience's belief in Qiu and Jiang's victory was strengthened.

Won the Shanghai Open Doubles Tennis Championship

(Right) Lin Baohua (Left) Zheng Zhaojia (Photo by Wang Kai)

Reverse Goes Smoothly

After the third game, Qiu and Jiang's military morale was slack and their techniques were careless. They thought that fate belonged to them and seemed that they did not need to reject people thousands of miles away. Unexpectedly, Lin and Zheng fought hard against the water and were determined to restore their fate. Heaven rewarded their ambition and they succeeded in succession. Therefore, in the six games after that, Lin and Zheng turned the reverse smoothly and were invincible. As a result, they won with six to two. The score is shown on the left.

Finals (Five Shots)

Fourth Set... Six to Four

Another Scene

Lin and Zheng regained a set, and their morale was greatly comforted. Between offense and defense, they felt like they had come to life. In the first two games, Lin and Zheng repeatedly won. At that time, Qiu and Jiang cheered up, hoping to complete the task as soon as possible to avoid failure. Therefore, in a flash, it became a two-two tie again. After that, the situation was very tense. At first, Lin and Zheng took the lead with three to two, but suddenly Qiu and Jiang took the lead with four to three.

Eternal Regret

Qiu and Jiang had already gained the advantage of taking the lead, and it was appropriate to take advantage of the situation to complete the success. However, after a little hesitation, they became an eternal regret. Lin and Zheng were full of color and skill, and they succeeded in succession in three consecutive games, that is, they won the fourth set with six to four.

Fifth Set... Six to One

Turn Defeat into Victory

Both sides had equal wins and losses, and the championship belonged to whoever had the upper hand in this final scene. Lin Baohua was as lively as a dragon and tiger, and his shots were all wonderful. Zheng Zhaojia was careful and lively. Jiang Daozhang's techniques were chaotic, and Qiu Feihai's long-term strength was insufficient. The situation of each other gradually became clear during the exchange of shots. Lin and Zheng became better and better in the battle, while Qiu and Jiang were too decadent to bear. In the end, Lin and Zheng won with six to one, which felt quite easy. The score is shown on the left.

Awards Ceremony and End of the War

The war came to an end and the awards ceremony was held. Chairman Hu Xiansheng gave a speech and invited Mr. Hu Yunlai to give the awards. Lin and Zheng stepped forward to receive the awards amidst the cheers of the crowd, and applause broke out to congratulate them on their success.

Heroes Each Have Their Own Strengths

The four heroes who played yesterday each had their own strengths. Lin Baohua's serve was the most powerful, ranking first among the four. His net was quite varied. His performance in the first two sets was mediocre, and he only showed his heroic qualities in the last three sets. Qiu Feihai's strength lies in his ability to handle the situation well. He can do it well regardless of the forehand or backhand, but his weak serve is his lifelong weakness. Jiang Daozhang's performance in the first two sets was wonderful and can be described as his proud work. It is a pity that his subsequent mistakes were repeated, resulting in a tragic defeat. His merits were not enough to make up for his mistakes, which is regrettable. Zheng Zhaojia's performance yesterday has fully demonstrated his tennis talent and will be a promising hero in the future. His skills can be called top-notch, and his long-term strength is also quite formidable.

Japan Sets New Record in Backstroke

Dentsu Tokyo, 10th. At the National Middle School Swimming Championships at the Meiji Jingu Swimming Pool, Mr. Katayama of Hamamatsu Middle School spent only 33.2 seconds in the 50-meter backstroke preliminary, setting a new Japanese record.

Important News

The Ministry of Education Explains the Qualifications for University Admission

The Ministry of Education issued an instruction to the Private Jinling University to explain the qualifications for university admission, stating that the qualifications for university admission must be graduation from a public or registered private senior high school. The so-called registered school refers to those that have been registered with the educational administrative authorities of each province and city and submitted to the Ministry for approval. The names of all private schools approved by the Ministry have been detailed in the appendix to the Ministry's Gazette, Volume 2, Issue 22. All private schools that have not been listed in the appendix, regardless of whether they have been registered with the education departments of each province and city, are not eligible to take the entrance examination for national, provincial, or registered private universities. Because many private schools in various places have been registered with the education departments of each province and city and submitted to the Ministry for filing, but have been returned for re-processing due to incomplete procedures, and have not been included in the appendix to the Gazette, in order to help the graduates of these schools to enter higher education, the universities are still allowed to refer to the previously issued list of public and registered private high schools in each province and city when enrolling students for the first semester of the 19th year, but this is limited to the first semester of the 19th year. Please comply with it.

Ministry of Education Explains Procedures for Registering Overseas Chinese Schools

The Ministry of Education, in order to explain the procedures for registering overseas Chinese schools, instructed the Guangdong Provincial Department of Education, stating that after reviewing the submitted report, it was found that overseas Chinese schools are different in nature from ordinary private schools within the country. The registration procedures should be handled in accordance with the revised regulations of the Ministry for registering overseas Chinese schools. Article 1 of these regulations states: "Any citizen of the Republic of China residing in another country who establishes a school in that location must submit a report and two copies of accompanying documents from the founder or their representative to the local consulate for forwarding to the Ministry of Education for approval and registration." According to this article, there is no requirement for an overseas Chinese school to first organize a board of directors when applying for registration. If a board of directors is established, it can be reported in the Ministry-issued board of directors information form at the time the school applies for registration, and there is no need to follow the procedures stipulated in the regulations for private schools. A copy of the regulations is enclosed for your information and compliance.

Free Talk

A Word of Advice

— Long

The power of promoting reading among women is far less effective than the ease with which the styles of dancing girls and prostitutes can attract their attention and imitation.

Learned people should not be arrogant towards the uneducated, because learning is not innate. If you had not had the money to study when you were young, wouldn't you be just as ignorant as them?

Money, if used well, can bring benefits; if used poorly, it can bring harm. The same is true of love between men and women.

Half of the prostitutes in the world are indeed forced by food and clothing, and the other half are misled by vanity.

Negative people often lament that the world is full of thorns and has no room for them, while optimistic people often stride forward with their heads held high, feeling at ease everywhere.

Don't bully him because you are stronger than him, beware of those who are stronger than you bullying you.

Relieving epidemics is not as good as preventing them, preventing them is not as good as hygiene, and hygiene is not as good as reading, because without reading, there is no way to talk about hygiene.

Managing price controls to benefit the poor is a temporary solution to an urgent problem. Improving agricultural affairs to increase production is a fundamental solution and a way to enrich the country.

Don't always take advantage of others. You must know that if there are no benefits to be gained, people will not let you take advantage of them.

On Hu Zijing

— Fang Er

During the recent occupation of Changsha by the Communist army, those in the educational circles with connections to the party and government all escaped, except for Hu Zijing, the president of Hunan University, who was unable to escape and reportedly died.

Mr. Hu, named Yuan Tan, courtesy name Zijing, was from Xiangtan. He once passed the provincial examination. In the late Qing Dynasty, he founded Mingde School in Changsha. Huang Kecheng, Tan Zuan, Wang Zhengting, and others all served in the school at one time or another. The school was established nearly thirty years ago and is the earliest and most famous private school in Hunan, especially known for Hu's ability to raise funds and travel to the north and south.

Hu was known for his grand words and also had a reputation for competence. He was nearly sixty years old with white hair and beard. The educational circles in central Hunan all respected him as "Mr. Hu Jiu," just as the gentry circles in Changsha respected "Mr. Yu Jiu." Mr. Yu Jiu, named Yu Gaoqing, courtesy name Zhihua, was killed along with Ye Dehui as a notorious local tyrant before the split between the Kuomintang and the Communists in Hunan. Now Hu has also died in an unnatural death. Friends in Beijing all said that Mr. Hu had been very influential in the educational circles in Hunan in recent years. After taking over as president of the university, he also wanted to be a member of the provincial government and often boasted of being a teacher of Chairman He Yunqiao. Perhaps this is why he was resented by the enemy, but it is not certain.

In recent days, many people have come to Beijing from Hunan to petition for rescue and relief, all saying that Mr. Hu Zijing was killed, Mingde School was burned down, and the neighboring Zhou Nan Girls' School was also affected. From then on, one of the most famous boys' schools and one of the most famous girls' schools in Changsha were reduced to ashes. It is regrettable. I have some free time in Beijing, so I write about it here.

Detailed Account of the East China University Summer Conference

— Xiao Meng

The so-called East China University refers to the six private universities in the Jiangnan region: Nanjing, Jinling, Soochow, Zhijiang, St. John's, and Shanghai. Over the years, they have organized summer conferences. Members include prospective bachelors, YMCA staff, and Ph.D.s, masters, and families with doctorates, totaling 58 people.

Dates: The conference was held from July 21st to August 3rd. From the 21st to the 26th, the meeting was held at Shanghai University. Initially, Dr. Toyohiko Kagawa, a Japanese labor activist, was invited to give a speech in Putuo, but Mr. Kagawa was unable to attend, so it was held at Shanghai University instead. At the time, the enthusiasm of the listeners was truly amazing. Just seeing the demeanor of a person like Toyohiko Kagawa was enough. On the 26th, they went to Putuo for a deeper discussion and returned to Shanghai on the 3rd.

Travel: This trip can be said to have implemented democracy. Both male and female students, as well as teachers and doctors, all stayed in the same cabin. Those on the same boat pointed and said, "This is a group of high-level civilians." In the evening, some used canvas beds, some slept on the floor. One person even brought an iron bed frame and slept high on the deck, which can be said to be special. The next morning, the boat did not provide breakfast, so groups shared food, filling the cabin. Each took out their bread, fruit, canned goods, etc. to satisfy their hunger for a while. There were about five teams, no different from the refugees on a desert island.

Conference: The conference venue was in Fayu Temple, also known as the Back Temple. It is strange that a Christian conference was held in a Buddhist temple. What is even stranger is that every time the meeting was held, all the monks listened without getting tired. Some say that this is because the abbot is broad-minded.

Lectures: Many well-known figures led the lectures this time, such as Dr. Jiang Hongqi from the Education Bureau, Dr. Shou Yicheng from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Dr. Luo Longji from Guanghua University and his wife, Mr. Pan Shaotang, a senior student who studied in England, Professor Zheng Ruogu from Labor University, and others. Each leader patiently taught, and all the students were willing to join the discussion. Among them, Mr. Luo, the political leader, was the most popular, and the most students joined his discussion group. There was also a British-style public debate on the topic of "Should China Adopt Democracy Today?" After the debate, a certain lawyer with a doctorate said, "Everyone must understand that the word 'today' means that democracy cannot be adopted in any way before 12:00 tonight." The audience burst into laughter, because this lawyer fundamentally argued that China could not adopt democracy today. There was also a new student who had just returned from the United States. Having grown up in the United States, this was his first time back in China. He did not understand the national language and suffered a lot at the conference. Whenever there was a long lecture, he always slept to enjoy himself.

Effective Proven Remedies for Summer Heatstroke

— Huang Weiyan

My kinsman, the venerable Mr. Shi Runyuan, is in his sixties and has been a vegetarian for decades. He runs a business in Xitang, Zhejiang, and is usually in good health. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the night the other day, he suddenly had severe abdominal pain. My aunt, who is known for her virtue, saw this and immediately asked Chinese and Western doctors to find a way to treat him, but to no avail. By nine o'clock the next morning, he had cramps in both feet and became unconscious. The situation was very critical. Later, he got a method from a friend. He burned brandy in a large bowl with a basin underneath, grabbed the fire with his hand and patted the cramping area to let the heat penetrate. The cramps stopped immediately, and he was able to turn danger into safety. If there are any of the above-mentioned heatstroke symptoms during this summer and autumn season, please treat them according to this method, which is indeed very effective.

Since the Tongle Amusement Park staged The Flying Dragon Biography, business has been booming. Poor Talk

— Zheng Yimei

Many literati are poor, hence Han Yu's work "Essay on Sending Away Poverty." I am also one of the poor scholars, experiencing the taste of poverty. Therefore, I have written some "Poor Talk" as follows:

Pawning is unavoidable for the poor. Among them, some people have the saying "To pawn and redeem is for the upper class, to pawn without redeeming is for the middle class, and to not pawn or redeem is for the lower class," as a way to make light of their situation.

A certain celebrity had a poem to avoid debt, saying, "Debts at the door are as chaotic as hemp, firewood, rice, oil, salt, soy sauce, vinegar, tea. I can't manage them either, so I walk out the back door to see the plum blossoms." Another New Year poem says, "The east neighbor sets up a feast to see out the old year, the west house opens a banquet to celebrate the new year. Only this old man forgets the taste of meat, a plate of tofu until the Lantern Festival." This is humor in poverty.

Good verses about poverty from the ancients, such as "Too poor, always afraid of people guarding against thieves, long illness, all suspecting that the dog is also a fairy," and "Pitiful, most of all, the girl pulling at her clothes, crying that the neighbor's lunch smells good," are extremely poignant.

There is a proverb, "If you are destined to be poor, you will always be poor, picking up gold will turn into copper. If you are destined to be rich, you will always be rich, picking up paper will turn into cloth," implicitly implying that people should not seek vainly. It is truly good advice.

"Eating in the stomach, wearing on the body" is also a proverb. Some people reverse it, saying, "Wearing in the stomach, eating on the body," which is an even deeper level of poverty. The original clothing has long been turned into ashes, and the remaining clothes on the body are still waiting to be pawned for rice.

A modern saying, "No carriages or horses at the door is elegance, having qin and books is not poverty." Poor but refusing to say poor, how elegant, how broad-minded.

The newspaper once carried a story about a poor scholar who often pasted dozens or hundreds of layers of old newspapers to make a thick quilt. When it became dirty, he would tear off a layer. As he tore it off, it became thinner and thinner, and the seasons had already changed from winter to summer. He claimed that it was in line with the climate and hygiene and boasted of the success of his plan.

What You Need to Know About Dancing (Part 1)

— The Crane That Doesn't Dance

Mr. Kael, a Russian who is proficient in the art of dancing, was met by a reporter yesterday at the Tchachunko Garden Cafe on Avenue Joffre. They talked at length about this topic, and since there are many people learning to dance these days, I have recorded the general outline of what he said below. He said that the art of dancing has been passed down since ancient times and can express personal emotions and human thoughts. Therefore, artists often use dance postures as models for copying. In the past, the famous Greek Pythagorean Academy used dance postures to explain psychology. Music can also use dance steps to express the spirit of the music. From this, we can see the great significance of the art of dancing. Psychologists have said, "You can know a person's education by listening to their words." The same is true of dance. You can know a person's style by looking at their dance posture.

The art of dance can be divided into three categories: (1) folk dance and traditional dance, (2) stage dance and arena dance, and (3) social dance. Social dance is the dance used in social circles. Entertainment in human life is an extremely important thing in life. It can be used to rest the brain and cultivate temperament. Although there are many forms of entertainment, dancing is the most beautiful, just as schools have gymnastics and sports. The function of dance is very great. Not only can it create a suitable physique and a beautiful posture, but it can also please the temperament and make the movements beautiful and the spirit healthy. Therefore, those who are proficient in dancing are often physically strong, long-lived, and not easy to age, because other sports are not as natural and appropriate as dancing.

We often think that dancing is an easy thing, resulting in poor posture and vulgar movements, which greatly affect a person's character. Therefore, when learning for the first time, you must consult a specialist or someone who is proficient in dancing to do basic exercises. Familiar with simple steps, you will be able to master them naturally over time. Then, when you enter the social arena, you will be able to handle them easily, be welcomed, and be admired.

Mr. Liu Shuofu of Shen Bao has been researching dance for a long time and has told me the following etiquette that should be known about dancing:

(1) When asking a female guest to dance, the first time it is appropriate to choose someone who is closer to you, the next time you should ask the female guests who are respected in the entire room, and then other ladies. Because asking to dance is to show respect, first asking a close female friend shows love and avoids other misunderstandings. Next, asking respected guests shows respect. Other than that, it doesn't matter, but you must pay attention. If the male guests each have their own close partners, it seems inappropriate to ask them to dance many times. You must also know that when there are fewer male guests than female guests, you must not let one or two female guests be disappointed. Most female guests want to leave the last dance to their lovers, so you should be aware of the situation and not insist on it, because most ladies use this last dance to resolve all the matters of the next appointment with their lovers. (2) It is appropriate to ask to dance after the music starts and one or two couples have already left their seats. Then, silently assess the female guests in the room and choose those who seem to want to dance but have not yet been asked by anyone. First, ask with a sincere and gentle attitude whether they are tired and whether they can dance with you. After their permission, stand up, leave your seat, walk to them, and move the chair for them (as you do when sending them back to their seat after the dance). Walk into the dance floor with them calmly and start dancing calmly and generously. Your attitude should be noble and lively, and you should avoid being coy. (3) If you must ask a certain female guest to dance, you may as well make an appointment in advance, wording it something like, "May I have the next foxtrot or Boston waltz with you?" and so on.

Warmth in My Heart (251)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Sows Good Fortune and Gets a Diamond Ring, Only This Fate Has the Heart to Sing the Golden Thread

After a few more weeks, their fundraising tickets with paintings, calligraphy, and antiques as prizes were finally issued. Although many family treasures were unwilling to be donated as prizes, for the sake of relieving the disaster victims, everyone had to part with a little. In order to encourage people to buy tickets, they had to give people something good. Therefore, the top prize included something like a masterpiece of the Four Wangs. Fortunately, those who bought that kind of ticket were all elegant and fond of antiques. Moreover, in order to encourage ticket buyers, there were many small prizes. Those small prizes were all gifts of recent paintings and calligraphy, and some were very exquisite. Approximately one out of every five tickets had a small prize. As a result, many people bought them. Zuo Shichen also bought a dozen tickets. He did not get the big prize, but he got several small prizes. On the other hand, Shi Guanping's Shen Gao's Collection of Famous Paintings was also published volume by volume. Because he himself was proficient in Zheng Qian's three perfections, so-called poetry, calligraphy, and painting were all good, and he was also a connoisseur, the printed products were naturally extraordinary. Sometimes, he even went to the factory himself to supervise the two Japanese technicians. If he encountered a poorly printed one, he would immediately reject it. Originally, printing those collotype editions was not the same as ordinary printed products. Ordinary printed products are printed by machines, only caring about speed, like using a rotary press to print newspapers. A small book can be printed in tens of thousands or hundreds of thousands of copies. The collotype edition only seeks perfection and does not seek speed. It is half-manual and seeks to be exactly like the original version. Copperplate printing cannot do this, so Shi Guanping rejected any that were slightly distorted in order to avoid damaging the true traces. Since the publication of this collection of famous paintings, not only could beginners learn from models and increase their knowledge, but those connoisseurs and collectors did not necessarily have to see his true works. At least they could get a rough idea from the collotype print. Therefore, after the publication of this collection of famous paintings, it became popular at home and abroad. All domestic artists had one copy. Later, not only was it popular domestically, but Japan, which has always admired Chinese painting, also searched for our ancient paintings for a year and bought them at high prices. They did not know how much they bought. As long as people were willing to sell, they spared no effort to collect them. Now that they saw the printed collection of Chinese famous paintings, they all came to buy them. Therefore, every collection of famous paintings was immediately reprinted in three editions. The sales were really good. Since the success of the collection of famous paintings, Shi Guanping has also printed various inscriptions on stone tablets on the calligraphy side, using good paper, good ink, and the same as the original version. All kinds of fonts are all chosen by himself. If he likes to write in that style, he chooses that one to copy. Not only are they sold in private schools, but they are also sold in schools. Therefore, their career in this bureau is also thriving.

Commercial News

Financial Gold Market Extremely Mediocre Last Week

Multilateral Constraints Cause Fluctuations and Peace

The gold market situation last week was very peaceful, the wind was calm and the waves were quiet, but the latent weakness had broken the eighty-two mark. From the beginning of the week to the end of the week, only twelve or thirteen taels were exchanged. Looking back, people still seem to be confused and there is no consensus in the industry. At the beginning of the week, the daily fluctuations were still eight or nine taels, but later they only fluctuated by three or four taels. However, recently, the multilateral forces have been mutually constrained and the trends have been opposed. As for the silver bars and silver prices, they were quite mediocre. The European market was stagnant, and even drafts and other advance orders have not moved for ten days. Therefore, the gold market has not changed much. The general circling situation since Wednesday was caused by the sale of Yuansheng Dai Luo et al. which once suddenly fell to seventy-two taels and two cents. On Friday, Hengxing Fuchang and other bulls pulled up sharply, and it rose sharply to eighty-four taels and nine cents. Until the weekend, it showed fatigue again. As a result, it was seventy-seven taels and a half, which was three taels and one cent lower than the previous Saturday. According to the daily exchange rate increase, it was sixty taels less. However, the current route was because the customs investigation was strict, so there was no corresponding receiving owner, and the price was five or six taels to seven or eight taels more than the period. The general situation of these five days from Tuesday, April 5th to 9th (Saturday) (August 4th, Monday, was also closed for one day due to the bank holiday) is described in detail below.

Latent Weakness Drops Three Taels and One Cent

On the 5th (Tuesday), there was no British silver market, but the telegraph of the previous day had already shown a decline. However, the draft did not move. The bank's internal market was firm first and then weak, which led to the initial opening of the September gold bid to rise two taels to eighty-two taels and seven cents, followed by eighty-four taels and a half. Afterwards, the selling households were active, and it was about to plummet by ten taels. In the afternoon, it was flat and closed at seventy-seven taels and one cent, which was three taels and a half lower than the previous weekend. The next day, the large silver bar returned to length, and the advance order did not change. The internal market was flat and then strong, while the gold price was soft in the morning and firm in the afternoon. The market once broke through the eighty-tael mark and closed back to seventy-nine taels, still rising about two taels. However, the total fluctuation for the day was nine taels. On Wednesday, the market situation was peaceful and there was only a fluctuation of three taels. The entry and exit of each firm were different, but the silver market and advance orders did not change. The internal market seemed tight, and the closing was seventy-nine taels and three cents. The next day, the silver market still did not change, and the draft was firm in the morning and flat later, which was contrary to the gold market. The gold bid hovered around eighty taels. From the initial flatness to strength in the morning, Hengxing, Yuanmao, Yongyuanheng, Fuchang and others pursued purchases, so in the afternoon it reached eighty-four taels and nine cents. Afterwards, each firm tended to sell, and the trend reversed sharply, breaking the eighty-tael mark, and the height was also six taels. On Saturday, the large silver bar and advance order did not shrink, and the gold market only fluctuated by three taels. In the early market, it was seventy-nine taels, and then Hengxing and others competed to buy it, and it once broke out of eighty taels. However, the seller was quick and Qin Kangrun still sold. As a result, it closed at seventy-seven taels and a half, which was three taels and one cent lower than the previous Saturday. The difference in one week was only twelve taels and seven cents, which was not the huge change of the previous week. Securities: Government Bonds Rebound Significantly Last Week

Customs, Reorganization, Disbandment Each Up Four to Five Yuan

Market Conditions Improve, Turnover Reaches Over 50 Million

Last week, the local bond market's futures turned bullish, and market sentiment was lively. Except for the first two days of the week, which were quiet with daily turnover of only 5 million yuan, the turnover on Wednesday and Thursday each reached 8 million yuan. The market was even better on the weekend, with daily turnover reaching 12 million yuan. The total turnover for the entire week was 50,011,500 yuan, exceeding the previous week's 26,670,000 yuan. Customs and Reorganization bonds were both buoyant, and Disbandment and Rehabilitation bonds also performed better than before. In addition, spot transactions for the entire week amounted to 87,700 yuan. The changes in bond prices were quite significant, unlike the sluggishness and lack of change in previous weeks. On Monday, market sentiment was still weak, and the trend continued to decline. However, except for the September Disbandment bonds, which fell by 1.5 yuan, there were no other major fluctuations. On Tuesday, although there was a slight recovery, only the September Disbandment bonds rebounded by 1.5 yuan, with no other changes. From Wednesday onwards, the market situation suddenly changed. Due to optimistic political situation, the Hunan affairs gradually settled, and there were some positive turns in the military situation in Shandong and Henan. Market sentiment improved, and investment purchases became smoother. The bond market phenomenon changed accordingly, and bond prices rose step by step. On Wednesday, each bond rose by 60-70 cents to 1.7-1.8 yuan. On Thursday, Reorganization and Customs bonds rose by about 1 yuan, and other bonds rose by about 50 cents. On Friday, the upward trend was the strongest. Customs and Disbandment futures jumped by more than 3 yuan, and Reorganization continued to rise by more than 2 yuan, also up about 1 yuan. On the weekend, the market was initially strong, but later, due to the eagerness of those settling accounts in the market, it began to ease. As a result, there were no major changes, and it was generally up 1 to 4-5 yuan compared to the previous week. Only the demand for 96 Financial bonds in the market was very low, and the price continued to be slightly weak. Yarn and Cloth: Yarn Sales Exceptionally Enthusiastic Last Week

Guangdong Merchants' Purchasing Power Strongest... Standard Nearly as High as Distant Delivery

The actual sales of cotton yarn were exceptionally brisk last week. Guangdong merchants were particularly eager to search the market, and all 10-count coarse yarns were purchased by them. Fortunately, the bottom stocks of 16-count and 20-count yarns were still available, and various factories were very willing to sell them according to the market trend, so the rising trend did not intensify. However, after the large-scale absorption of Japanese 20-count "Ri Chang" (立馬), "Lan Feng" (藍鳳), and "Hong Xi" (鴻禧) yarns by Guangdong merchants, there was a shortage of goods and the market became tight. Considering the development of autumn sales and the strong purchasing power of Guangdong merchants, colleagues opened up to Japanese factories. All Japanese yarn futures for January, February, and March of next year were sold out, mostly in the hands of colleagues and customers. The yarn market is currently in the autumn sales season, and this huge amount of actual sales provides a solid foundation. However, the cotton industry in various countries around the world is still in decline, and a large increase is feared to be difficult to achieve. According to statistics, various merchants bought a total of 26,225 bales throughout the week, of which one-third or two were futures. It is said that most of the purchases by Guangdong merchants were transferred to warehouses for storage and contained speculative elements. In terms of prices, 10-count native yarn rose, 16-count and 20-count yarn rose slightly, and 20-count Japanese yarn tended to rise. The buying power for standard yarn became stronger, and most people predicted that the Gengtian rice harvest would be abundant this year, and autumn sales would be prosperous. There were quite a few buyers, and each month exceeded 160 taels. On the weekend, due to the U.S. cotton government's estimates favoring short positions, 3-grade yarn plummeted by 6-7 yuan, and market sentiment softened slightly. Prices for each month fell back by 1-2 taels. As a result, the price for the near month was the same as last week, and the price for the distant month rose by about 1 tael. The total turnover for the entire week was 98,350 bales. The following is a record of the purchase amount of each merchant:

Merchant　Bales　Amount　Merchant　Bales　Amount　Merchant　Bales Amount

Cotton Market Suffers Setback Last Week

Demand for Spot Cotton Extremely Weak

The cotton market was very weak at the beginning of the week. The weather was favorable, and the new cotton production was good. Later, there was a report of drought in U.S. cotton, but the telegraph prices were still flat. However, local sentiment was unanimously bullish, and the bulls heavily increased their positions. The Ningbo merchants were particularly strong. Rui Da, who was originally a short, covered all of his 20,000 dan short positions on Wednesday and Thursday and turned into a 20,000 dan long position. The market price was greatly shaken, breaking through the 5 tael mark. However, the sales of spot cotton were completely stagnant, and most factories absorbed enough cotton due to the low price of Indian cotton. There were few inquiries, and even Japanese factories occasionally purchased only a small number of bales. Before the report, the bulls vigorously raised prices because U.S. cotton production was within 14 million bales, and many even expected it to be around 13.5 million bales. Unexpectedly, the government estimates were beyond everyone's expectations. U.S. cotton fell by more than 60 pounds, and the Shanghai market plummeted by 60 cents. Rui Da closed out 14,000 dan of its long position on Saturday. The market price will have to follow the fluctuations of U.S. cotton. The Shanghai Exchange's standard rose first and then fell, resulting in a drop of 1-2 cents compared to the previous week. The total turnover for the entire week was 300,000 dan. Japanese merchants entered futures contracts for 23,980 dan. Yao cotton arrived at 1,520 bales, and firms entered 1,680 bales. The following is a record of the purchase amount of manufacturers and firms: Manufacturer Purchases Highest Price Lowest Price Turnover Deadline

U.S. Cotton Rebounds, British and Egyptian Cotton Continue to Fall

Yesterday, U.S. cotton initially strengthened due to good news from Liverpool, but then weakened due to Wall Street sell-offs. Finally, it rose again due to purchases by colleagues. Futures rose by 5-6 pounds, and spot rose by 5 pounds. British cotton futures fell by 1-2 points, and spot fell by 29 points. Egyptian cotton spot fell by 40 points. Indian cotton market closed.
