Past and Future of the Cotton Market

The cotton market was slightly stable in the first half of this year due to the sharp changes in exchange rates and the lack of sources and thin inventories. However, the actual situation was still dull because Indian cotton was cheap and there was a large demand for it. Furthermore, factories, in response to social needs, changed to producing finer count yarns and adopted higher quality American cotton. The following is a list comparing the changes in cotton futures in the past six months with the same period last year:

First Half of This Year　Same Period Last Year

Highest　Lowest　Highest　Lowest

January　36.55　34.45　33.50　32.45

February　36.00　34.80　33.75　32.90

March　35.70　34.35　34.45　33.05

April　35.65　34.95　33.30　30.10

May　35.65　34.65　33.25　30.55

June　37.40　35.20　32.25　30.55

Half Year　37.40　35.95　35.30　30.55

Judging from the above table, the market price this year is higher than last year, which is purely due to the stimulation of the exchange rate market. American cotton, which dominates the world cotton market, was low last year, as was Indian cotton. Although foreign cotton fell, the combined price was still high, so it advanced and retreated in inverse proportion to foreign cotton. The following is a comparison of U.S. and Indian cotton market prices:

New York U.S. Cotton Spot　Mumbai Broach

This Year　Previous Period　Last Year　Same Period　This Year　Previous Period　Last Year　Same Period

Highest　Lowest　Highest　Lowest　Highest　Lowest　Highest　Lowest

January　17.55　16.25　20.55　19.95　309　287　363　315

February　16.90　14.90　20.80　19.85　282　252　363　352

March　16.45　14.00　21.65　20.70　270　243　382　369

April　16.80　15.85　20.75　19.40　272　249　369　326

May　16.70　16.20　19.90　18.10　265　247　353　325

June　16.15　13.25　19.05　18.30　248　201　348　335

Half Year　17.55　13.25　21.65　18.10　309　201　382　325

The cotton market in the past six months has been as described above. I dare not rashly predict future trends, but in my opinion, there is little optimism. Let me briefly explain. U.S. cotton's sales have decreased and inventory has increased, causing the market price to gradually fall below 13 cents. According to the government's first estimate, there are 45,815,000 acres of new cotton fields, and the number of abandoned fields is still included. If we take the average rate of abandoned fields in the past ten years, 3.6%, as a ratio, then the actual harvested area will be more than 44 million acres. Based on the average yield of 158 pounds per acre in the past ten years, the future harvest will be approximately 14 million bales. With a production of 14 million bales and the current state of the world's cotton industry being in decline, it seems that the supply and demand situation is out of balance. If the world cotton industry continues to be sluggish without any signs of recovery, and the worry of increasing inventories remains, then the predicament of the U.S. cotton market seems difficult to resolve. As for Indian cotton, the domestic revolutionary atmosphere is strong, and cotton mills work intermittently, leading to a sharp increase in inventories. Although there are reports of floods affecting the progress of the new cotton crop, most of it is still good. Without drastic changes, it seems impossible to quickly develop the market price. The situation of domestic new cotton is generally good in various provinces, except for the remote provinces of Henan and Shaanxi. If the climate is suitable, a medium harvest can be expected. According to a survey, the inventory of raw cotton in various factories in the local area at the end of the first half of the year was approximately 834,000 dan. The following is the supply and demand situation during the six months: Consumption in the First Half of the Year Inventory at the End of June

Chinese Cotton 123,0820 319,390

U.S. Cotton 510,150 177,460

Indian Cotton 619,500 348,730

Other 15,520 8,360

Total 2,375,990 853,940

Judging from the above inventory, it is enough to supply two and a half months of consumption in the second half of the year. However, the weather is hot, and the work efficiency of various factories has decreased. Moreover, due to business reasons, there are frequent reports of factories suspending work or reducing work. Therefore, this inventory supply should last for more than two and a half months. Moreover, foreign cotton has not yet arrived, and the amount is also huge. Looking at the sluggish transaction of spot cotton and the sparse transaction of new cotton in the market in recent days, we can see the general environment of the cotton market. The future trend can be roughly understood. However, changes in exchange rates and trends in the yarn market also have considerable influence (August 3rd Agricultural Report).

Grain: Downriver Rice Market's Falling Trend Slightly Calmed

Zhabei

Yesterday, the number of rice boats arriving in Shanghai at various docks was less than ten, and market sales were slightly active. Therefore, the falling trend of Northern Non-glutinous rice stabilized slightly. High-quality goods maintained their original prices, while medium and lower-quality goods were slightly weaker by half a cent because all buyers focused on high-quality Northern Non-glutinous rice, and no one inquired about goods below the middle level. The trend was stable. Although the arrival of Dongxin Non-glutinous rice was not smooth, the overall market price fell by half a yuan again, opening at only 19.5 yuan. The Thin Rice market was quiet, with only a few ships occasionally arriving at the port, but the sales were not good, and the price was still stable. The price of new top-grade rice on the Luli Road suddenly tightened, so there was no significant impact on the local market. However, according to reliable sources, several ships will arrive within a few days. The Baiyuan market was uneventful, transactions were not active.

South Shanghai

The number of ships arriving from downriver has decreased. Although the factories and warehouses here are eager to sell machine-milled Non-glutinous rice, there is a tendency to sell in batches. Therefore, the situation of Changbang machine-milled Non-glutinous rice has gradually stabilized. The situation of Sutong Non-glutinous rice is inconsistent because there are inquiries about high-quality goods in small quantities, while no one inquires about medium and lower-quality goods. Therefore, the overall market price fluctuates by one cent. This type of goods has been very scarce recently, and the situation is quiet. As for the association's evaluation, it has little effect during this period of weak goods. Transactions can still be made, but the source is not large, and the market is stable.

Local News

New Rice from Zhoupu on the Market

Harvest is Considered Bountiful

People's Hearts are Greatly Settled Because of This

New rice (named "Dong Xin") produced in the Zhoupu area of Pudong has been on the market for several days. The quantity arriving each day is only thirty or forty shi, but it is all unpolished rice, milled white by rice mills such as Xinchang and Shenli. The initial opening price was twenty-one yuan per shi, and yesterday it opened at twenty yuan. Rice shops in the northern and southern markets purchased wholesale in an endless stream, and it is sold at retail in the southern market to meet the market demand. Since the new rice from Pudong has been on the market, the rice industry in Shanghai has been sending letters one after another to inquire about the situation of the harvest, with the intention of investigating the harvest. Yesterday, the rice industry received a letter from the rice industry in Zhoupu reporting that most of the new rice in the four rural areas has been harvested this year, and the harvest is considered bountiful and the quality is good. However, the fields near the river and in low-lying areas have not yet been harvested, and it is observed that the harvest will not be reduced. This time, the typhoon did not damage the fields. Harvesting in the Minhang area will take another ten days. The rice industry received this news, and people's hearts are settled because of this. The new rice produced in areas such as Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, and Wuxi (named "Xi Xin") is the largest in quantity. The harvest of their new rice is expected to be around the Double Ninth Festival, when it may be seen on the market.

Many are Asking to Maintain the Affairs of the China Merchants Bureau

Some are Asking the Acting Director-General Cai to Return to His Post Immediately

Some are Asking Chairman Li to Come Forward and Maintain the Critical Situation

Telegram from the Union of Employees of the Head Office

Supervisor Wang of the China Merchants Bureau Employees' Union Bitterly Pleads for Cai's Acting Director-General's Return to His Post. The National Government Specially Appointed the Committee for the Reorganization of the China Merchants Bureau to Exercise Its Powers, and Supervisor Wang Xunjian. The Commercial Bureau Unfortunately Suffered a Sudden Major Change, and Former Director-General Zhao Suddenly Died. All Employees of the Bureau are Deeply Saddened and Mournful. Immediately Upon Receiving Your Order, They Were Instructed to Continue to Work as Usual and Not to Abandon the Bureau's Affairs. The Day Before Yesterday, They Received an Order from Your Ministry to Forward the Chairman's Order, Especially to Continue Actively Reorganizing and Proclaiming to All Staff to Comply. We Deeply Admire Your and the Chairman's Profound Care for the Commercial Bureau and Empathy for the Employees. Everyone Was Inspired Upon Hearing the Order. However, the Recent Situation Within the Bureau Has Been Worsening Since Acting Director-General Cai Hastily Returned to Beijing. The Average Daily Expenditure, Such as Steamer Coal, Ship Berths, Salaries, and Office Expenses, is at Least Ten Thousand Taels or More. Debt Interest is Not Included. If There is a Shortage of One or Two Operations, They Will Have to be Suspended, and Affairs Will Be Difficult to Maintain. However, the Daily Income That Can Be Relied Upon is at Most Three or Four Thousand Taels, a Huge Difference, Which is Becoming Increasingly Difficult. In Addition, the Bureau Has No Officially Responsible Person, and Its External Credit is Weak. If This Situation Continues, the Salaries of the Crew Will Be Cut Off, and the Supply of Coal Will Be Cut Off, Then the Suspension of Navigation and Work Stoppage Will Be Inevitable. All Employees Have Repeatedly Thought and Unanimously Believe that at This Time of Heavy Military Transportation, in Order to Uphold Your Excellency's Purpose of Protecting Navigation, in Addition to Urgently Hoping That Acting Director-General Cai Will Return to His Post Immediately and Officially Take Office, There Should Be a Responsible Person to Maintain the Situation During This Transition Period. The Only Perfect Plan is to Appeal to Your Excellency to Order the General Management Office and the Board of Directors to Bear Joint Responsibility and Vigorously Maintain Operations and Facilitate Military Transportation Before the Government Appoints a Candidate, So That the Pressure of External Debt Can Be Eased, the Urgent Needs of Internal Daily Use Can Be Raised, Military Transportation Will Not Be Suspended, and Then the Government's Successor Can Also Calmly Find a Candidate. Moreover, in Terms of the Bureau's Finances, the New Appointee Will Hopefully Have All Parties Working Together Harmoniously to Help Support the Overall Planning, Relieve Future Difficulties, and Start a New Opportunity for Reorganization. In Short, the Government Has Its Own Authority in Hiring and Administrating Personnel, and What Dare the Employees Say? Only the Employees Are in the Bureau and Have a Deeper Sense That the Bureau's Affairs Cannot Be Without a Master for a Day, and Operations Cannot Be Interrupted for a Moment. Therefore, They Offer Their Thoughts and Contribute Their Humble Opinions. Whether They Are Appropriate or Not, We Hope That You Will Consider and Issue an Immediate Order. Respectfully, the Union of Employees of the China Merchants Bureau of the Special Municipality of Shanghai Bows Respectfully.

Letter to the General Management Office (Board of Directors) Requesting to Maintain the Bureau's Difficulties and Urging the Payment of Back Wages. Respectfully, Since the Unfortunate Murder of Former Director-General Zhao, We Have Read Your Office's Announcement, Your Association's Letter, the Supervisor's Telegram, and the Ministry of Transportation's Order to Forward the Chairman's Order, All of Which Instructed All Employees to Continue Working as Usual and Continue to Work Hard. Our Association Members Obeyed the Order and Strove to Maintain the Bureau's Affairs and Protect the Current State of Operations. However, Upon Quietly Observing the Recent Situation, We Gradually Felt that Hidden Dangers Were Arising. Although Acting Director-General Cai Hastily Returned to Beijing, Secretary-General Wang Was Appointed to Temporarily Represent the Bureau's Affairs to Avoid Abandoning Them, But in Reality, Difficulties Are Indeed Unavoidable. The Daily Income is Only Several Thousand, but the Expenditure Exceeds Tens of Thousands. Coal and Ship Salaries Are in Urgent Need. Any Mistake Will Hinder Operations. If Acting Director-General Cai Cannot Return to the Bureau Within Days, or Even if He Returns, There Is Still No Remedy for Funds. Then Not Only Will the Bureau's Dockworkers' Salaries Be Unsettled, and Life Will Be Alarming, but Also It Is Feared That Daily Quotations Will Be Announced and Coal Will Not Be Supplied, and Operations Will Be Suspended. The Precarious Danger Cannot Be Denied. Our Association Deeply Understands the Central Government's Sincere Concern for Navigation and Takes Into Account the Importance of Transportation. We All Believe That the Employees of the Weekend are in a Position to Advise and Save the Urgent and Maintain the Danger. The Telegrams Have Been Urging and Supervising. In Addition to One-Sidedly Telephoning the Supervisor to Urge Acting Director-General Cai to Return to the Bureau as Soon as Possible to Take Charge, We Believe That During This Transition Period, Your Office (Your Association) Should Jointly Maintain, Raise Daily Use, Preserve Operations, and Pay Off Back Wages Together with the Board of Directors and the General Management Office, So That the Difficulties Can Be Overcome and Reorganization Can Be Hoped For. We Believe That Your Office (Your Association) Must Share the Same Concerns About the Safety of This Bureau and Console the Employees' Expectations and Live Up to the Government's Past Protection of Navigation. In Addition to Separately Writing to the Board of Directors (General Management Office), We Specifically Send This Letter to You, Hoping for a Reply. Respectfully, the Union of Employees of the China Merchants Bureau of the Special Municipality of Shanghai. August 9.

Appeal Telegram from the Nine Shipping Associations

The Nine Shipping Associations Telegraphically Submitted to the National Government in Nanjing, Chairman Jiang of the National Government, President Tan of the Executive Yuan, and Minister Wang of the Ministry of Transportation. We Humbly Report That Since the Assassination and Death of Director-General Zhao of the China Merchants Bureau, All Affairs of the Bureau Have Become More Chaotic. Former Minister Wang of the Ministry of Transportation Appointed Cai Pei as the Acting Director-General, but It Is Said That He Has Also Resigned Now. Therefore, There is a Lack of People in Charge, and the People's Hearts Are Even More Alarmed. The Bureau's Affairs Will Inevitably Be More Disruptive. If There is No One Who is Usually Trusted to Come Forward and Maintain the Critical Situation, Then the China Merchants Bureau Will Inevitably Go Bankrupt. Needless to Say, China's Shipping Industry Has Always Relied on the China Merchants Bureau as the Only One. If It Goes Bankrupt One Day, Then China's Shipping Industry Will Be Greatly Affected. Ten Thousand of Our Colleagues Will Also Lose Their Jobs, and What Can We Imagine for the Future? The China Merchants Bureau Originally Had a Board of Directors. Now, at This Critical Moment, How Can We Let It Be Free and Carefree and Not Make Efforts to Maintain the Critical Situation? Moreover, Chairman Li Has Been in the Bureau for Many Years, and He is More Careful About the Bureau's Affairs and is Respected Both Internally and Externally. If He Can Come Forward and Maintain the Critical Situation, Then He Will Be Able to Succeed Easily and Achieve Twice the Result with Half the Effort. Our Association and Other Colleagues, For the Sake of the Country's Shipping Industry and For the Sake of Our Colleagues' Livelihoods, Dare to Telegraphically Submit to Your Majesty to Quickly Order Chairman Li to Make the Effort to Maintain the Critical Situation in Order to Emphasize the Shipping Industry and Follow Public Opinion. This is Truly a Blessing. We Humbly Present This Urgent Order and Await Your Instructions. Respectfully, the Joint Office of the Nine Shipping Associations in Shanghai, the Maritime Federation Association, the Shipping Association, the Yan Ying General Association, the Nan Jun An Association, the Bei Jun An Association, the Yan Ying General Association, the Joint Association of Drivers, the Shan Zheng Industry Association, and Others Bow Respectfully.

Quezon's Mission to the United States

He Passed Through Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday and Set Sail Yesterday Morning

The Zi Lin Daily Reported That Quezon, President of the Philippine Senate, is Going to the United States While Ill to Resolve the Tense Situation. Yesterday (the 9th), He Passed Through Shanghai on the Japanese Empress Ship. Due to Illness, He Stayed in the Ship at Wusongkou and Did Not Land. Quezon Left Manila on the McKinley President Ship on the 2nd of This Month and Transferred to the Japanese Empress Ship After Arriving in Hong Kong. According to His Words, He is Determined to Go to the United States This Time. He Will Not Return Home Until the Tense Situation Between the United States and the Philippines is Finally Resolved. After He Arrives in the United States, He Will Meet with President Hoover to Discuss Everything. The Current Tension Between the United States and the Philippines Has Been Unseen for Many Years. He Especially Opposes President Hoover's Appointment of Roosevelt Nicholas as the Deputy Governor of the Philippine Islands Because Roosevelt is Known for Opposing Philippine Independence, and His Measures Will Inevitably Fail to Live Up to the Expectations of the Filipino People. Quezon Was Quite Ill When He Left the Philippines This Time, So He Took His Whole Family and a Doctor With Him. However, After Being Cared for by the Sea Breeze, His Illness Has Greatly Improved. According to the Japanese Empress Ship, She Set Sail for the United States Yesterday Morning.

Land Bureau Urges the Collection of Land Practice Certificates

Zhu Yan, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau, Issued a Proclamation Yesterday, Saying, "For the Purpose of Proclamation, It is Investigated That the Land of Each Household in the Twenty-Fifth Bao and Sixteenth Tu of the South Shanghai District (East to the Huangpu River, South to Youche Matou Street, Xuejia Bang Road, South District Street, Zhao Jia Wan Street, Small Stone Bridge Street, Qiao Jia Road, West to Xun Dao Street, Lao Bai Du Street, and East to Xianji Road in the Inserted Flower Land, South to Fumin Lane, Hongqiao Lane, West to Fu Jia Street, and North to Hua Jin Road) Has Been Surveyed by This Bureau. It is Urgent to Issue Land Practice Certificates to the Owners of the Tu. It is Appropriate to Issue a Proclamation to Inform the Owners of the Tu to Quickly Pay and Collect It. This is a Special Proclamation."

Freight Bills and Packages Do Not Have Stamp Duty Affixed

Letter from the Transportation Office to the Transportation Company

The Transportation Offices of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Sent Letters to Various Transportation Companies Yesterday, Saying, "The Case Investigates the Method of Affixing Stamp Duty to Books and Vouchers at Various Stations. It Was Notified in This Office's Notice on July 2 of This Year. Yesterday, We Received a Letter From the Finance Department of the Ministry of Railways on July 11, Saying, 'Respectfully, We Have Recently Read Your Office's Notice Regarding the Method of Affixing Stamp Duty to Books and Vouchers at Various Stations. Except for the Regulations in Items Two, Three, and Four, There is Nothing Inappropriate. Item Five, the Freight Bill, is Only a Voucher for Picking Up Goods and is Not a Receipt for Money. Item Six, the Package Ticket, Belongs to Cargo Transportation According to the Case and is Not Within the Scope of the Regulations. Neither the Railway Bureau Nor the Merchants Need to Affix It. We Should Correspond and Ask You to Check and Correct It and Hope to Order It to Be Notified Accordingly.' In Addition, We Received a Letter on July 26, Briefly Saying, 'Approved by the Office's Vehicle Character No. 1388, Regarding Whether or Not Items of Freight Bills and Package Tickets Should Be Notified and Deleted, the Ministry Will Discuss With the Tax Bureau for Approval Before Another Method Will Be Implemented, Etc.' The Case Involving Whether or Not Stamp Duty Should Be Affixed to Items of Freight Bills and Package Tickets Has Been Approved by This Ministry and Approved by the Ministry of Finance to Temporarily Exempt It From Affixing. It Was Ordered in the Order of the Ministry of Finance No. 3829 on March 28 of This Year. Various Kinds of Books and Vouchers, Whether They Were Previously Affixed With Stamp Duty or Not, That Are Not Within the Scope of These Regulations Should Be Allowed to Stop Completely. In Addition to Informing the Ministry of Finance to Order Various Stamp Tax Bureaus to Comply With the Order, It Is a Special Joint Order to Comply With the Case. The Affixing of Stamp Duty to the Two Items of Issuing Bills and Package Tickets Should Be Immediately Handled by Your Office to Issue a Notice for Deletion Without the Need to Discuss With the Tax Bureau for Approval. The Previous Letter Was Sent in Response, Hoping That You Will Check and Order It to Be Notified Accordingly, Etc. Upon Receiving This, We Jointly Issued a Notice to Order Various Transportation Companies and Various Related Staff to Be Fully Informed."

The County Government Received Instructions From the Provincial Relief Association

The Shanghai County Government Received Instructions From the Jiangsu Provincial Relief Association, Saying, "For the Purpose of Following Orders, the Case Received a Telegram From the Relief Committee, Saying, 'In Recent Years, Disasters Have Spread Everywhere, and the People Have No Means of Livelihood. We Look Up at Zheng Xia and Sigh With Our Roofs Up. The Poems Sing of Sad Wild Geese, and We Cannot Provide Even Crumbs of Grass. This is Truly a Catastrophe That Has Never Been Seen Before. Those Who Care About the People's Suffering Cannot Help But Feel Deeply Worried. It Is Said That This Year's Rainfall and Sunshine Have Been Timely, and Wheat and Grain Will Be Reported to Have Been Harvested, Which is an Opportunity for Heaven and Human Affairs to Turn. Whether the Sweet Rain Has Been Widespread in Your Province, How Much is the Amount of Water and Dry Land, and What is the Harvest? The Counties Under Your Jurisdiction Must Have Detailed Reports. This Association is in Charge of Relief and Rescue, and We Are Not Proud of the Past Disasters, But We Wish for the Future Harvest. We Respectfully Hope That You Will Order That the Amount of Rainfall in Various Places This Year, As Well As the Amount of Wheat and Grain Harvested, Be Listed in Detail and Sent in a Letter, Etc.' In Addition to Distributing It, It is Appropriate to Order the County Chief to Comply With the Detailed Listing and Reporting in Order to Verify and Forward This Order, Etc." County Chief Yan Has Already Transferred the Order to Various District Chiefs to Quickly Investigate and Report in Order to Compile and Forward It, It Is Said.

Initiating the Organization of a Flat-Price Rent Promotion Association

The Inaugural Meeting Was Held Yesterday

Thirty-One Members of the Preparatory Committee Were Elected

Citizens Zhang Yichen, Yu Hualong, Etc. of This City Initiated the Organization of a Rent Dispute Mediation Committee. Details Have Been Recorded in Yesterday's Newspaper. It is Now Known That the Association Held an Inaugural Meeting in the Auditorium of the Shuji Elementary School Near the Tianhou Palace Bridge Yesterday. More Than 150 Representatives of Various Groups Attended. Hu Shouqi, Yu Hualong, and Gu Wensheng Were Publicly Elected as the Presidium. After Performing the Ritual, the Chairman Reported the Purpose of the Meeting. Then, Representative Jin Chuxiang, Etc. Gave Speeches, and the Discussion Began Immediately. (1) Determining the Name of This Association, the Resolution Was Revised to Be the Shanghai Flat-Price Rent Promotion Association. (2) Appointing the Formal Preparatory Committee, It Was Resolved to Appoint Yu Hualong, Zhang Henghai, Hu Shouqi, Sun Mingqi, Gu Wensheng, Xu Huimin, Li Ruzhang, Shen Zhongying, Wang Wei, Zhang Yichen, Jin Chuxiang, Cheng Guichu, Wang Chengdong, Wu Peiyin, Weng Guangda, Ye Qichang, Cai Xiaohe, Wang Jingzhai, Wang Pingnan, Cheng Kefan, Chen Jiaxuan, Zhu Baoluo, Li Henglin, You Lanjie, Yu Zhende, Shao Yuerun, Yu Mingxun, Chen Wewen, Jiang Xianhe, Zhang Zilian, Ye Zhisheng, and Other Thirty-One People as Members of the Preparatory Committee. (3) Appointing Drafters to Draft the Constitution of This Association, It Was Resolved to Appoint Zhang Henghai, Hu Shouqi, Sun Mingqi, Yu Hualong, and Wu Peiyin as Drafters. (4) Deciding on the Preparatory Expenses of This Association, It Was Resolved That Each Member of the Preparatory Committee Would Temporarily Advance Five Yuan. (5) Deciding on the Location of the Association, It Was Resolved to Hand It Over to the Preparatory Committee. (6) Deciding on the Date of the First Preparatory Meeting, It Was Resolved to Appoint Comrade Yu Hualong to Be Responsible for Convening the Meeting. After the Meeting, Tea and Snacks Were Served, and the Meeting Was Adjourned.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks for Exemption From Pen and Ink Tax

Document Submitted to the Ministry of Finance

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submitted a Document to the Ministry of Finance, Saying, "The Pen and Ink Trade Association Continues to Ask for Pen and Ink to Be Exempt From Tax. We Respectfully Submit the Circumstances and Ask for Your Review and Approval. The Case Investigates the Previous Request From the Shangzheng Association to Exempt Pen and Ink From Tax. On July 1, We Received a Reply From Your Ministry, Which Said That the Pen and Ink Paper Is Not Only Limited to Education and Documents, Which is Different From Purely Educational Supplies. Now That Various Kinds of Paper Are Subject to Customs Duty, Pen and Ink Are Treated the Same Way, So It Is Not Appropriate to Exempt Them Alone. However, It Is Said That Each Hundred Jin of Huizhou Ink Only Sells for Forty-Four Taels of Silver. If This is True, Then the Current Export Tariff of Imposing Four Taels of Customs Silver Per Hundred Jin Is Too Heavy. In Addition to Copying and Sending It to the National Tariff Commission When Revising the Export Tariff in the Future to Investigate and Revise It to Achieve Proper Compliance, It Is Appropriate to Notify You. After the Association Received It, the Association Sent a Letter to Forward It. Now, on the 7th of This Month, We Received Another Letter From the Pen and Ink Trade Association, Which Said That We Humbly Read the Ministry of Finance's Reply That Pen and Ink Paper Is Not Only Limited to Education and Documents, Which is Different From Purely Educational Supplies. We Thought That Although Schools Also Lecture on Western Learning, They Never Fail to Learn Chinese First. Since We Learn Chinese First, All Citizens' Reading and Writing Must Grasp a Pen to Research. Then, Pen and Ink's Assistance to Education is Parallel and Not Contrary. Moreover, the Government Advocates Education Without Leaving Any Efforts. Books Are Exempt From Their Customs Duties, and All It Wants is for Books to Circulate Throughout the Country. The Depository of Books Is in Writing, and the Silent Writing of Words Is in Pen and Ink. Now That We Advocate Domestic Goods, Pen and Ink Are Naturally in the Example of Advocating. The Association Thought Again and Again That the Raw Materials of Books Are in Paper. If Paper Is Not Made Into Books, Then It Will Be Subject to Half the Tax, and If It Is Made Into Books, Then It Will Be Completely Exempt From Tax. And the Raw Materials Required for Pen and Ink (Such As Wool, Bamboo Sticks, Yellow Wolf, Rabbit Skin, Printing Materials, Smoke Gum Tablets, and Musk) Are Collected From Remote Provinces and Foreign Countries. In the Mainland, They Pay Local Tax Levies, and at Customs, They Pay Import Taxes. Before and After, It Has Exceeded 20%. However, the Book Tax Is Only on Its Raw Materials and Does Not Tax the Books. Pen and Ink's Assistance to Books for Education Is Proposed to Be Similar to the Request for Documents. It Seems That There is Nothing Inappropriate. Moreover, the Material Taxes Have Been Repeated to the Extreme. That Is to Say, the Statistics of Pen and Ink Sales Are Only 500,000 Yuan Per Year. If We Calculate 10% of the Annual Sales Amount for Tax, It Will Be as Much as 50,000 Yuan. If We Calculate With Customs Silver, It Will Probably Be Only 30,000 Taels. The Request to Refer to the Example of Documents to Exempt Tax Is Only Like Reducing a Grain of Rice in a Warehouse. It Seems That It Does Not Hinder the Public's Financial Support. We Should Report the Circumstances and Ask the Ministry of Finance to Approve the Exemption From Tax According to the Example to Relieve Merchants' Difficulties and Benefit the Students, Etc.' After the Association Received the Pen and Ink, Although It is a Semi-Educational Supply, According to Its Nature, It Seems That It is Also Different From the Paper That is Only a Raw Material for Educational Supplies. Since Imported Goods Have Been Imported, the Effect of Domestically Produced Pen and Ink Has Gradually Decreased, and Sales Have Shrink. With Products of 50 Million Yuan, the Workers Who Rely on It for Their Livelihoods Still Reach More Than 3,000 People, and the Relationship is Not Insignificant. Even If We Only Talk About Supporting Domestic Goods and Maintaining Manual Livelihoods, the Tax Exemption Situation Is Similar to That of Artificial Hand-Woven Native Cloth. Moreover, According to the Production Amount for Tax Calculation, the Public Tax Revenue Donated by Tax Exemption is Minimal, Which Does Not Hinder Financial Support. Since the Association Has Sent a Letter to Ask, It is Inconvenient to Block It From Above. We Should Prepare a Document Again to Ask Your Ministry to Review and Approve It According to the Example to Help Maintain It. We Are So Grateful. Sincerely."

These Were Originally Ordinary Events. Unexpectedly, the French Imperialist Capitalists Were Violent and Willful. First, They Refused Mediation and Regarded Our Country's Government Offices as Nothing. Then, They Hired White Russian and New Workers to Persist in Their Goal of Destroying the Workers. Finally, They Showed Their Teeth and Claws, Arrested the Workers, and Eventually Evolved Into the Massacre of Workers on July 21. The Means Are Getting More and More Brutal, and the Plans Are Getting More and More Ruthless. The So-Called Conditions Show No Sincerity and Are Deliberately Delayed Day After Day. Since This Is the Case, It Is Impossible to Conceal Anything. Our China Has Not Yet Reached the Time of Extinction. The Concessions Are Just a Kind of Leased Land. They Have Been So Cruel and Poisonous in Dealing With Us Chinese. If We Do Not All Rise Up to Make a Strong Representation to the French Imperialists, I am Afraid That the Failure of the French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Will Be Enough to Promote Our National Subjugation. In Other Words, the Problem of French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Is Not a Local Problem. It Can Be Said That It Is the Entire Problem of Our Chinese Nation. A Small Number of French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Can Be Their Sacrificial Lambs. Why Can't the Compatriots of the Whole Country Be the Sacrificial Lambs of the French Imperialists? We Are Now Helping the French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers to Seek Survival for the Entire Nation and Also to Avenge the Humiliation of the Whole Nation. If the French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Do Not Achieve Their Final Goal, Our Responsibility Cannot Be Discharged for a Day. Our Responsibilities Are (1) to Seriously Warn the French Imperialists and Urge Them to Wake Up as Soon as Possible. (2) To Use Economic Power to Help the French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Fight to the End Without Yielding. (3) To Awaken the Compatriots of the Whole Country to Take a Unified Stance and Launch a General Attack Order Against the French Imperialists to Make Them Afraid to Despise Our Nation. We Hereby Declare and Pray for Your Public Appraisal." The Congress of Representatives of Various Trade Unions in Shanghai to Assist the French-Funded Water and Electricity Workers Declaration.

Legal French Water and Electricity Workers' Warning to Senior Management

The French Water and Electricity Workers' Union yesterday planned to issue a written warning to senior manager Monsieur, as previously reported. We understand that the union's warning letter has been drafted and was sent out yesterday afternoon. We have obtained the original text, which is as follows: Warning Regarding: It is known that this time, the workers of our union, due to unbearable pressure on their livelihoods, had no choice but to propose demands. These demands were peaceful and moderate, and none exceeded normal limits. Your Senior Management, however, issued three notices, sternly rejecting them, which inevitably led to a strike and disappointed the workers. This is the first point for which we must issue a warning. Before the strike occurred and after it had already started, our government authorities convened mediations twice. Your Senior Management disregarded these, and your stubborn attitude is already appalling. This is the second point for which we must issue a warning. Furthermore, on July 8th and 11th, our union workers accepted Mr. Du Yuesheng's mediation within a possible range and immediately returned to work. However, Your Senior Management suddenly changed its mind, reneging on its previous commitment. First, it closed the iron gates to prevent entry, and then it refused to have the new workers withdraw. This resulted in the failure of our workers' return to work. This shows that Your Senior Management lacks sincerity in negotiations, allowing the strike to gradually escalate and the situation to become tense, leading to the tragic incident of July 21st. This is the third point for which we must issue a warning. Recently, the central government has shown concern for the labor movement and has separately engaged Mr. Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, and the City Party Headquarters to make every effort to mediate so that the strike can be resolved in a good way. However, the various conditions accepted by Your Senior Management not only failed to provide the workers with satisfaction and had many defects, but also created additional problems beyond the original subject of the conditions, wanting to dismiss a large number of workers (reduced from 150 to 40). This kind of additional problem is not only ridiculous but also absurd. Not only is it difficult for our union workers to accept, but all 800,000 workers in the city will also deny that Your Senior Management is deliberately prolonging the strike, with a dangerous and unreasonable intention. This is the fourth point for which we must issue a warning. In summary, regarding these four points, Your Senior Management cannot evade its responsibility for this strike and must bear a major responsibility. Our union hopes that Your Senior Management will realize this as soon as possible and prevent the strike from escalating and prolonging, leading to further unexpected events. We have no choice but to issue a serious warning to Your Senior Management.

Relief for the Cotton Textile Industry

The Municipal Government, based on a report from the Social Affairs Bureau, forwarded to:

The State Council for investigation and action, as ordered by the National Government

The National Government issued an instruction to the Executive Yuan on the 7th, regarding the Shanghai Mercerized Cotton Textile Industry Association's request for the allocation of subsidies for relief: "Instruct the handling of this matter. The Shanghai Municipal Government reported that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce stated that the Shanghai Mercerized Cotton Textile Industry Association wrote, 'Our industry peers all believe that the cotton textile industry is declining day by day and is difficult to maintain. Since last winter, nearly half of the factories have closed down, and the remaining factories are mostly precarious. We have formulated six proposed solutions: (1) Revise labor-management conditions in the shortest possible time. (2) Reduce and exempt harsh taxes and levies. (3) Request the National Goods Bank and the Municipal Bank to provide interest-free loans. (4) Request the government to allocate subsidies. (5) Request the government to order all government agencies to use domestic goods. (6) Request Zhejiang Province to abolish harsh taxes on yarn and cloth. All have been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for separate relief. Except for the third proposal, which has been ordered by the Ministry of Finance to be handled by the National Goods Bank, and the fifth proposal, which has already been addressed by the Municipal Government, we implore your association to forward the remaining proposals separately.' It was found that the industry's request for relief, except for the third item regarding the exemption of heavy levies by the Zhejiang Provincial Tax Bureau, which was expedited due to the time limit, has already been telegraphed by our association directly to the Ministry of Finance and Zhejiang Province. There are still the first item, which is under the jurisdiction of your bureau, and the fourth item, which should be submitted by the bureau to the Municipal Government and then to the National Government. Therefore, this bureau has submitted a plan to the cotton textile industry for relief to your government, which has been forwarded to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to consult separately with the Ministry of Finance to reduce taxes and order the National Goods Bank to discuss and implement various proposals. Now, according to the association's report, the cotton textile industry's proposed relief plan still has the first and fourth items, requesting your approval. Regarding the fourth item, requesting the government to allocate subsidies, citing the precedent of the National Government's relief for the shipping industry by allocating public bonds, we request the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to allocate 2 million yuan of reorganization or demobilization bonds to be distributed by the Cotton Textile Industry Association according to the amount of inventory in each factory for relief. This matter concerns the national treasury and should be submitted with a document to your director for review and forwarding for approval and implementation. Therefore, this city's mercerized cotton textile industry is indeed declining day by day and is difficult to maintain, which is a real situation. The request for the allocation of subsidies for relief concerns the national treasury. In addition to instructing the waiting for submission for review and approval, it is appropriate to report the situation and request your prompt instruction to comply, which is for public convenience. Therefore, in addition to instructing knowledge of the notification to be handled by the Executive Yuan, it is hereby ordered that the Yuan examine and handle this matter, which is hereby ordered."

Suggestions on the Scope of Rejecting Foreign Goods

Proposed by Xu Chunrong

Consisting of Eleven Categories

Quarterly member Xu Chunrong of the China National Goods Maintenance Association, in view of the crisis of gold being expensive and silver being cheap, with China facing the risk of bankruptcy, believes that the fundamental solution lies in unifying and reforming the currency system and promoting local industry. The immediate solution should be a nationwide rejection of foreign goods to reduce leakage and maintain the lifeblood of the nation. Therefore, he specifically proposed to the association a scope of rejecting foreign goods, consisting of eleven categories, all of which have Chinese substitutes, and requested that it be forwarded to the Party and government authorities for adoption and supervision of public groups to implement. The original text of his proposal is recorded as follows: "Regarding the proposal, this association was established more than twenty years ago as a pioneering group in promoting national goods. From the beginning of our comrades' union, we deeply knew that the result of the free sale of foreign goods is that money flows abroad, and the people's livelihood is cut off in society. The country has no way to stand, and the people have no way to live. Unfortunately, in the past twenty years, the free sale of foreign goods is like a dyke collapsing, which cannot be resisted. The people's livelihood is declining like a river, going down a thousand miles. Although the voice of promoting national goods continues to appear in metropolitan centers, few respond to the high-sounding tune. Or some take promoting and improving national goods, developing overseas trade, and resisting imports as a prerequisite, which is indeed a fundamental talk. Evidenced by the current situation in our country, the knowledge of the technical community is backward, the financial power has been manipulated by foreigners, the shipping power has also been controlled by foreigners, and the knowledge of merchants in international trade is naive. Moreover, the policies of various countries to protect their own domestic industry and commerce are becoming more and more sophisticated. It is easy to talk about seeking a place in the commercial war by competing with them with our backward cause, that is, chasing a hundred steps with one step. It is necessary to know that gold is expensive and silver is cheap. Our China, which uses silver, should take the increase in the cost of foreign goods and the decrease in the cost of exports of national goods as a good opportunity for China to revitalize its industry. However, the failure of national goods to sell as usual and the decline of the export business are even worse than before. Although the import of foreign goods has temporarily shown a slight pause, the report stated that Japan's goods shipped to China in the past month have returned to their original position. One country is like this, and other countries can be known. The so-called new national goods in China all draw materials from foreign raw materials, so the cost of national goods cannot escape the value of the source of foreign goods. The Chinese people's use of foreign goods has become an unbreakable habit. If it is not foreign goods, it seems that it is not suitable for the needs of life. The so-called promotion of national goods has become an impossible environment to realize its goals. Today's flooding of foreign goods in China is like a collapsed dyke. If the breach is not urgently blocked, there will be nothing left for the fish. The method of blocking the breach is to choose the most needed, most popular foreign goods, and the original Chinese goods can be used instead, refusing to use them regardless of their invasive nature. Hold on to the purpose of foreign goods and make compatriots across the country refuse to use them. Then the violent leakage can be blocked immediately, and the operation of national goods can be developed immediately. There is no failure to obtain the final success. Think about the industrial and commercial policies of various countries, promoting them abroad by invading, and blocking them at home. The Chinese industrial and commercial policies are promoted abroad. Customs cannot exempt export taxes, and merchants have no long-term vision and ability. That is, there is no way to promote foreign goods. Foreign goods are imported into China. Customs cannot protect taxes by force, and the people are addicted to foreign goods. This is a way to resist the import of foreign goods. Even with foreign goods and textiles, the Chinese population is 500 million. Each person buys 2 yuan of foreign textiles every year, then the money flowing out of the country should be 100 million. Only this kind of leakage is enough to be shocking. There are still endless consumption of foreign goods. The great leakage can be known. If we Chinese people can work diligently in this regard, in a blink of an eye, imports will definitely turn into exports. What is the benefit to the country? Now, taking it as a self-determination method to awaken the people to uniformly refuse to use foreign goods, this high-minded and reasonable work will definitely have a quick effect. Now, the major foreign goods that can be rejected and used with original substitutes are listed as follows: 1. Foreign goods' textiles 2. Foreign goods' cotton yarn 3. Foreign goods' rayon 4. Foreign goods' cigarettes and foreign wines 5. Foreign goods' kerosene 6. Foreign goods' soap 7. Foreign goods' aquatic products 8. Foreign goods' sugar 9. Foreign goods' cosmetics 10. Foreign goods' porcelain 11. Foreign goods' coal The above eleven items are the scope of propaganda to reject foreign goods. Products manufactured by foreign businessmen in factories established in China are regarded as foreign goods and rejected as an example. The propaganda method to reject them should be determined that this association is the China National Goods Maintenance Association, which unifies the power and actively proceeds to report to the Central Party Department for approval and dispatch personnel to guide, and report to the Central Party Department to order party departments at all levels across the country to cooperate with local agencies to guide the agricultural, industrial, commercial, and academic groups to organize Chinese national goods maintenance sub-associations within seven days after the document arrives and widely promote. Each week, there will be at least two publicity events. Regardless of the poor villages, there must be lectures on the advantages and disadvantages of promoting national goods and rejecting foreign goods wherever there are people. Each month, there will be at least one door-to-door promotion. Party and government personnel bear the heavy responsibility of leadership, and they must set an example. Party departments at all levels are responsible by standing committee members to supervise the staff and party members under their jurisdiction. After receiving three publicity events, they are not allowed to use the above-mentioned foreign goods again. If violations are found or supervision is weak or condoning offenses, the supervisory committee will discuss the punishment. Government agencies are responsible by the chief officer to supervise the various agricultural, industrial, commercial, and academic groups under their jurisdiction. The standing committee members are responsible for supervising the schools under their jurisdiction. The principals of the schools are responsible for supervising them. The managers of companies, businesses, and factories are responsible for supervising them. If violations are found or supervision is weak or condoning offenses, the local party department will investigate and discuss the punishment. If supervision is effective and actual results are found, the local party department or public group will provide proof and submit it to the central government for generous rewards to encourage and punish. As for the fundamental method of promoting national goods, this association will properly draft opinions and submit them for implementation. Is it feasible? I respectfully ask for a public decision. This is to the China National Goods Maintenance Association, proposer Xu Chunrong."

A List of Agricultural Statistics in Shanghai

Investigation of Major Items

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in view of the fact that the development of industry should start with the investigation of farmers, specially sent several investigators to various districts last year to conduct detailed investigations on the main items of farmers. The report compiled from the investigation is now being published in the bureau's social monthly, which will be issued in the near future. Here is an excerpt of the statistical results compiled into a list so that those who care about rural society can get a sneak peek: (1) Owner-cultivators account for about 35.0%, semi-owner-cultivators account for about 33.6%, and tenant farmers account for 31.4%. (2) Farmers engaged in sideline occupations account for 90%, of which those engaged in weaving account for 3.09%, those engaged in embroidery account for 3.3%, those engaged in craftsmanship account for 43.4%, those engaged in commerce account for 12.5%, those engaged in education account for 2.6%, and those engaged in public office account for 7.3%. (3) The number of people receiving education is relatively high, with owner-cultivators accounting for 33.0%, semi-owner-cultivators accounting for 25%, and tenant farmers accounting for 13.0%, with an average of about 23.7%. (4) The average number of acres of cultivated land per person is 1.8 acres, with owner-cultivators averaging 2.2 acres, semi-owner-cultivators 1.8 acres, and tenant farmers 1.2 acres. (5) The average price of farmland is 239 yuan per acre, with the highest being 1,200 yuan and the lowest being 60 yuan. (6) In terms of farmers' housing, tile houses account for 84.3%, thatched houses account for 10.0%, and tile houses with thatched houses account for 5.7%. (7) Comparison of the number of livestock breeding households: (1) Cattle: Owner-cultivators account for 51.7%, semi-owner-cultivators account for 38.0%, and tenant farmers account for 10.3%. (2) Sheep: Owner-cultivators account for 23.4%, semi-owner-cultivators account for 36.6%, and tenant farmers account for 40.0%. (3) Pigs: Owner-cultivators account for 54.7%, semi-owner-cultivators account for 38.1%, and tenant farmers account for 7.2%. The average price of livestock is 73 yuan per head for cattle, 3.03 yuan per head for sheep, 14.7 yuan per head for pigs, 0.73 yuan per head for chickens, 0.79 yuan per head for ducks, and 0 yuan per head for geese. (8) The average annual wage for agricultural workers is 108 yuan, the monthly wage is 13.5 yuan, the daily wage for men is 0.5 yuan, and the daily wage for women is 0.3 yuan. (9) Comparison of the cultivated area of main crops: cotton accounts for 34.8%, rice accounts for 21.3%, wheat accounts for 20.6%, soybeans account for 8.5%, broad beans account for 4.1%, vegetables account for 4.4%, and other miscellaneous crops account for about 6.3%. (10) The average yield per acre is 308 jin for rice, 62 jin for cotton, 108 jin for soybeans, 160 jin for wheat, and 114 jin for broad beans. (11) The average price of crops per 100 jin is 4.03 yuan for rice, 14.96 yuan for cotton, 4.53 yuan for soybeans, 3.73 yuan for wheat, and 3.40 yuan for broad beans. (12) Comparison of capital: Owner-cultivators' land capital accounts for 78.1%, housing capital accounts for 19.5%, and operating capital accounts for 2.4%. Semi-owner-cultivators' housing capital accounts for 32.3%, operating capital accounts for 3.7%, and land capital accounts for 64.3%. The overall average is that land capital accounts for 73.3%, housing capital accounts for 23.7%, and operating capital accounts for 3.0%. (13) The number of indebted households: Owner-cultivators account for 55.5%, semi-owner-cultivators account for 78.7%, and tenant farmers account for 72.3%, with an overall average of 68.6%. (14) The average amount of debt per household: Owner-cultivators have 509.7 yuan, semi-owner-cultivators have 321.9 yuan, and tenant farmers have 104.5 yuan, with an overall average of 312.0 yuan. (15) The reasons for borrowing are 13.6% for construction, 38.5% for daily use, 46.9% for weddings and funerals, and 1% for indemnity. (16) The interest rates on loans: 7.4% are interest-free, 2.3% have a monthly interest rate of 1%, 20.6% have a monthly interest rate of 1.5%, 10.4% have a monthly interest rate of 2%, 2.1% have a monthly interest rate of 3%, 2.5% have an annual interest rate of 1%, and 54.7% have an annual interest rate of 2%. (17) The number of lending households accounts for about 5%, with an average of 87.8 yuan lent per household. (18) The average annual food expenses per household are 389.8 yuan for owner-cultivators, 293.1 yuan for semi-owner-cultivators, and 189.1 yuan for tenant farmers. The overall average is 290.7 yuan per household per year, or 41.5 yuan per person, accounting for 75.7% of total living expenses. (19) The average annual clothing expenses per household are 60.3 yuan for owner-cultivators, 26.7 yuan for semi-owner-cultivators, and 15.2 yuan for tenant farmers. The overall average is 33.8 yuan per household per year, accounting for 8.0% of total living expenses. (20) The average annual education expenses per household are 31.7 yuan for owner-cultivators, 8.0 yuan for semi-owner-cultivators, and 0.3 yuan for tenant farmers, accounting for 2.6% of total living expenses. (21) The average annual social expenses per household are 22.5 yuan, accounting for 51% of total living expenses. (22) The average annual living expenses per household are 399.4 yuan, with an average of 57.9 yuan per person. (23) The average rent per acre is 3.88 yuan, with the highest being 10 yuan and the lowest being 2 yuan. (24) The average tax per acre is 1.09 yuan, and the average tax per household is 12.6 yuan. (25) Comparison of rental systems: those paying in cash account for 95.5%, those paying in grain account for 2.2%, those sharing profits account for 2.2%, and those giving gifts account for 1.1%.

Nothing Is Too Strange In This World

Now she has opened her own brothel and accumulated a lot of ill-gotten gains. She has a daughter named Rong Ling. Since childhood, she has been betrothed to A Xiao, the son of a farmer surnamed Lu from the same hometown. She was brought to the Lu family as a child bride at the age of seven. Judgment of the Case of Mutual Accusations Between Hu Huilin and His Wife

Jockey Hu Huilin, when young, was married by his parents to Ms. Wenxian, the sister of Yong business Fang Jiaobai. They have been married for sixteen years and have seven children together, demonstrating their mutual affection. However, in the winter of the sixteenth year (of the Republic), the magician Lang Deshan brought his daughter Mina to Shanghai to perform. Hu was seduced by her beauty and began to resent his wife. Initially, they merely shared the same bed but had different dreams, then they drifted apart, and eventually they ended up in court. Hu claimed that Ms. Fang had taken medicine to induce an abortion and requested a divorce. Fang denied all of the plaintiff's claims and countersued, accusing Hu of abandonment and requesting that Hu pay her property worth 60,000 gold dollars for her living expenses and the education of their children. After repeated hearings, Hu, although far away overseas and represented by a lawyer, was ultimately ruled by Judge Yang that both parties' claims were without merit and were dismissed. Each party was to bear their own litigation costs. The reasoning of the judgment is recorded below: The plaintiff requests a divorce on the grounds that there is no affection between the two parties and that the defendant took medicine to induce an abortion. Marital discord is not comparable to a breakdown of affection. The plaintiff and defendant have lived together for more than ten years and have six or seven children. If there were no affection between them, how could they have stayed together until now? Therefore, his claim is clearly untrue. Regarding the claim that the defendant took medicine to induce an abortion, whether or not it happened, it is not sufficient reason to immediately request a divorce. The defendant argued that the plaintiff had an affair and intended to divorce and remarry, which is not without cause. Regarding the defendant's countersuit for alimony, the plaintiff left 2,000 dollars for household expenses when he went abroad to do business, and the defendant also took 3,500 dollars, which cannot be considered abandonment. As for his threatening to not return to the country, it was a moment of overreaction and cannot be used as evidence. Furthermore, temporary discord between husband and wife does not necessarily mean that they cannot reconcile. In order to maintain family harmony, the defendant should not demand 60,000 dollars in alimony simply because the plaintiff requested a divorce. Based on the above arguments, in accordance with Article 98 of the Civil Procedure Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text.

Woman Freed from Illegal Confinement in Shackles, Case Transferred to Court

Zhang Xushi (also known as Xu Xiuling), the wife of Zhang Genlin, a villager from Shenjiaxiang, Huatingtou, in the northeastern countryside of this county, was to be sold by her husband, but when he failed to do so, he locked her in a room with huge shackles on her feet, denying her food and drink. She and Jin'er were sisters in the same factory. Today she came to my place to play, and the clothes were also stored with me, not enticed. However, she has been having an affair with Zhu Hongxiang for more than a year, and now because she does not want to follow him, she has been appointed to Yu Yonglin's house and plans to escape to other places to break away from Zhu, which is true, etc. After obtaining the confession, Director Ren determined that the defendant Chen Yangshi had enticed a young girl to take clothes and planned to abscond together, which was undeniable, so he sentenced her to wait for a document to be transferred to the local court for trial today.

Adulterer Scares Away Husband

Sock Factory Partner Destroys Property

Continental Hotel Files Claim for Compensation

Dong Boqing, manager of the Continental Hotel on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, recently arrested Guan Xiongshu, a lodger, and sued him at the French Police Station, claiming that the defendant came with three or four young men to open room 326. Before long, Guan suddenly destroyed the dressing mirror, teapot, and other items in the room without any reason. Therefore, he was arrested and requested to be held accountable for the loss. The police chief approved the request and ordered Guan to be detained. The case was sent to the French Court for investigation the morning before yesterday. First, the plaintiff filed a complaint about the previous situation, and then Detective Ni Xiafei reported that he was dispatched by the police chief to investigate the whole story. The investigation revealed that the defendant, Guan Xiongshu, was a partner in a sock factory, earning more than ten dollars a month. Only four days after entering the factory, he had an affair with a female worker. The female worker's husband found out and caught them both. At that time, the defendant invited the female worker's husband and others to the plaintiff's Continental Hotel to open a room for mediation. When they arrived at the hotel, the defendant knew that the reconciliation was hopeless and unfavorable to him, so he became desperate and resorted to evil methods. He deliberately broke the dressing mirror and other items in the room, intending to scare them away. Sure enough, the husband was scared away, but the hotel refused to let it go because the defendant had destroyed the property for no reason and arrested him. Guan Xiongshu confessed to the above-mentioned circumstances, but stated that he only had more than 20 dollars and requested a grace period to compensate. Judge Zhu sentenced Guan to ten days in prison, suspended for two years, and ordered him to provide a guarantee and pay off the remaining losses within one month. The money paid shall first be given to the plaintiff to collect.

After a Prostitute Becomes Respectable, Her Romantic, Inferior Nature Remains

Wu Zhisun's Concubine, Namely Qian Huiqing

Moving Mahogany Furniture to Escape

Wu Zhisun from Tianjin is engaged in military uniform business in Shanghai and makes considerable progress. Because of this, he often indulges in prostitution. Last summer, he met a prostitute, Shihua, and they were deeply in love, pledging their love. The prostitute, named Fang, was from Xishan and was only 21 years old. Soon after, she withdrew her name from the prostitute register and returned to her original name of Qian Huiqing. Wu rented No. 840 Mengnala Road to hide her, spending more than a thousand dollars to buy a complete set of mahogany furniture and all necessary items. In addition, they agreed on monthly expenses of 200 dollars. At the beginning of her respectability, they were able to live in harmony, but after several months, her romantic and inferior nature gradually revealed itself. She often thought of leaving. On the 22nd of last month, while Wu was at his main wife's residence, Qian took the opportunity to move all the mahogany furniture away. When Wu returned home, the phoenix had already left the tower. After investigation, it was learned that Qian was hiding somewhere, so lawyer Zhan Jifeng was hired to sue the defendant in the Special District Local Court. The day before yesterday, the defendant was summoned to court and confessed that she had moved the mahogany furniture as accused by the plaintiff, but said that the furniture was purchased with her own funds and is now pledged by her. The plaintiff has nothing to do with it, and the plaintiff still owes her more than 2,000 dollars, etc. Judge Yang questioned the plaintiff, who completely denied the defendant's confession. The plaintiff's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, then requested that the owner or manager of the store selling the furniture be summoned to court to prove who purchased the furniture. Judge Yang agreed and adjourned the case, ordering the parties to prepare evidence for further questioning.

Concubine Sues for Division of Estate

Wife Expresses Unwillingness

After the death of a man named Jiang from Tongzhou, his successor wife, Gui, is now sixty years old and has two grown sons. Jiang also has a concubine, Lou, all living in their self-purchased home at No. 25 Tongzhou Road. However, Lou has no children, and the mother and sons of Gui treat her distantly, making it difficult to live together for a long time. On May 26th of this year, Lou quietly left. Gui not only did not try to persuade her to return, but widely published advertisements. Lou felt that this was too difficult to endure, so she filed a lawsuit in the Special District Local Court to divide the estate. She claimed that her husband's estate included a residence, 400 mu of fertile land in Kunshan, 20 rooms in Tongzhou, and 800 yuan in shares of the Yuanji Company on Fada Road in this port. She requested a division. The day before yesterday, the defendant, Jiang Gui, was summoned to court and testified that there were only 22 mu of land in Kunshan, only 46 mu and three bungalows in Tongzhou, and only 100 yuan left in the Yuanji stock. The family is large and it is impossible to divide the estate. Her eldest son also came to court and testified that he wished the plaintiff to return home to live and cook together, and they would support her until old age. He did not want to divide the estate. Judge Zhou questioned Lou, who confessed that it was truly unbearable and she did not want to return. The court asked her if the defendant denied having so much property, and since she was suing, she should present evidence to prove each item or state the exact location of the property so that it could be investigated. This cannot be accomplished with empty words. The plaintiff replied that the amount of property was what her late husband had said, but she did not know the locations and lacked evidence. After the lawyers of both parties argued, Judge Zhou ordered that the judgment be announced on the morning of the 13th of this month.

According to the Kuomintang News Agency, the Seventh District Party Department of this city yesterday submitted a report to the Municipal Executive Committee, stating that the court's announcement of the investigation results of the Zhang case was unexpected and aroused public indignation. It is found that Zhang Jinfeng, a local tyrant in Jiangwan, falsely encircled land and transferred it to foreign merchants. Since the municipal government ordered the Public Security Bureau to arrest him and transfer him to the Shanghai Local Court for punishment according to law, it has been a year, but there is no news of the outcome. Zhang Jinfeng was released on bail with a price of 50,000 yuan and is at large, proud of himself. Local people are worried that this case will not have good results, and rumors are rife. However, the colleagues of the department all believe that the court under the rule of the party is far from the era of warlords. Such a major case has extremely sufficient evidence, and the rumors on the road are definitely not credible. Now, the Secretariat of the Ministry of the Army has forwarded the correspondence between the Municipal Government and the Local Court, and it is learned that the case has been investigated by the Procuratorate of the Court and it is considered that a decision of non-prosecution should be made, which is unexpected. It is found that the errors in the disposition document have been severely refuted in the Municipal Government's application for reconsideration, and it is no different from being completely destroyed. Originally, there was no need to repeat it, but it is believed that the law should be fair and the government should respect public opinion. Zhang Jinfeng, in the name of encircling land, oppresses the villagers, and then changes the use of the land to mortgage foreign merchants. His crimes are obvious and cannot be concealed. He has been fortunate enough to escape the law under the rule of warlords for many years because of his money and power. Now, fortunately, the Municipal Government has clearly investigated and arrested Zhang and sent him to the court for punishment. Then, the gentlemen of the court should be fair and punish him according to the law to extend the law and make the people happy. Who knows that the investigation results only end with the five words of non-prosecution, how can it convince the people and show the party's spirit of the rule of law? Now, the rumors are spreading and public opinion is boiling, and public indignation is aroused. It is believed that the Party Department has the responsibility to supervise the government. At the time of the Municipal Government's application for reconsideration, this document is submitted to the committee for prompt transfer to the Local Court. It is requested that the gentlemen of the law enforcement should handle the case with a good conscience and not let the local tyrants steal the net, which is not only the good fortune of the villagers, but also the good fortune of the party's rule. Respectfully presented to the Municipal Executive Committee for hearing. The Municipal Executive Committee has transferred it to the Local Court after receiving the report.

Paint Industry

Due to the reorganization issue, the Shanghai Municipal Paint Industry Association's Steering Committee, the woodworking group industry, invited the reorganization committee members from all walks of life in the Chinese Concession to hold a preparatory meeting at Hongyunlou, Fadama Road, at 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. Those who attended included Zhang Fukang, Ling Youqiao, Ma Zhigang, Zhou Shanqing, Huang Shouchun, Xu Guoqing, and more than 20 others. Zhang Fukang was publicly elected as the chairman, and reported to the public the purpose of the meeting and narrated the past procedures. Min Xingchu, the document representative, made a statement, stating that since this association was ordered to reorganize, it has spared no effort in publicizing and guiding the fellow industries for half a year. It has only been achieved now that the association members have filled out the membership certificates and registered with the association. Although those who are clear-headed and enthusiastic about public welfare account for 80% of the people, there are still those who are located in the Chinese boundary and have a high reputation, and were members of the former public office era, the board of directors era, and who have turned a deaf ear to this reorganization matter, which is really incomprehensible. It is found that the reorganization procedures of this association will be completed soon, and the National Government requires that the industrial and commercial association law must be completed uniformly before August 16th, so the deadline has been chased, and the member list of each group will be sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to request a certificate of approval so that it can be reported to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for approval and the date for the establishment meeting can be set. However, on the 6th of this month, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce continued to send a letter saying that according to the law, it is still necessary to investigate the capital amount of the members' stores in various industries as the standard for the Chamber of Commerce to collect membership fees from the industry associations. If the capital investigation report is missing or omitted when reporting the establishment, it is considered that the procedures are incomplete and the certificate will be issued slowly. However, it is found that the number of fellow industries in this association is large and scattered in all walks of life in the Chinese and French Concessions. It is impossible to complete it without asking the leaders of each road to bear the duty of investigation. It is inevitable that the law will be enforced and the hands will be insufficient, and the deadline will be exceeded and subject to illegal punishment. It has already been reported to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce according to the facts and has not yet received a substantive reply. However, if the investigation of the capital amount is concentrated in Dongjie and Xiaonanmen, etc. in the city, which are the areas where woodworking stores are concentrated, the leaders of each family have repeatedly sent letters to invite them to visit and advise them, but they have turned a deaf ear, causing the rest of the fellow industries to follow the example of the major stores and hesitate to move forward and shirk each other. The superiors strictly ordered and urged them, and the subordinates deliberately delayed, which really made the people of this association unable to handle it and failed to achieve success. Therefore, it is requested that the gentlemen who attended the meeting plan to remedy it in order to facilitate the progress. After public discussion, it was decided to elect another representative to go to advise and avoid delaying the progress. Next, the reorganization committee Zhou Shanqing, Ling Youqiao, the guest Lin Zhizhou lawyer Huang Hanxiang, etc. all gave speeches, and the reorganization and establishment of the paint association was detailed and clarified, and everyone was moved. Then, it was publicly agreed that the major issues such as the investigation of the capital amount to be handled before the establishment should be borne by the people who came to the meeting separately to fulfill their duties, and everyone agreed. After the discussion, a banquet was held until the stars shifted before everyone dispersed happily.

Yarn Factory Workers Union

The Preparatory Committee of the Federation held its second preparatory committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Zhou Ziyang reported on matters (omitted) Discussion items (1) The registration section proposed that the union registration form has been drawn up, please amend the case. Resolution passed and approved. (2) The labor dispute in the Pudong Yarn Factory has not been resolved for a long time. This association intends to request the Municipal Party Department to send a letter to the Social Affairs Bureau to convene both parties for mediation as soon as possible to seek an early resolution. Is it rich to ask for a public decision? Resolution to hand it over to the Document Section to prepare a document and request handling. (3) The standing committee member proposed whether it is appropriate for this association to publish a letter to the yarn factory workers, please make a public decision. Resolution passed. (4) It is found that there are many yarn factories in Hudong. This association should set up an office to facilitate the progress. Resolution to appoint Comrade Huang Hualnan to take charge. (5) Is it appropriate for this association to send personnel to investigate the factory numbers and worker numbers of factories in various districts, please make a public decision. Resolution to recommend Huang Jinan and Bao Cai Keguang to be responsible for the investigation in Hudong, and Zhou Zhonghua and Wang Ruiting to be responsible for the investigation in Huxi. (6) It is found that the staff of this association is insufficient for distribution, and six voluntary secretaries should be appointed for distribution. Resolution passed. (7) It is found that the two committee members, Ju Qianzhang and Wu Fuxing, have not come to the meeting to work. The Municipal People's Training Association should be informed to let the two committee members come to the meeting to work on a daily basis to facilitate the progress. Resolution to hand it over to the Document Section to prepare a document for handling.

(2) The resident standing committee member will go to the company to negotiate the rice subsidy issue. (9) The Sichuan Factory Union's dispute will be announced by the Propaganda Department of this union.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that there will be showers on the coast here. The weather between the mouth of the Yangtze River and Kyushu Ryukyu is extremely bad, with a violent cyclone due to the hurricane moving northwest, north, or north. There is a strong northeasterly wind in the Yellow Sea. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 95.4 and the lowest was 77.4. On the same day last year, the highest was 90.5 and the lowest was 77.7.
